\section{Explicit \(m=1\) Same-Shell Non-Enriched Coefficient Extraction}

\section{Short explanation}

The only genuinely non-automatic benchmark-side slot in Step IV is the same-shell non-enriched sector.
In the minimal truncation \(m=1\), this sector is already reduced to an explicit \(2\times2\) Hermitian matrix problem.

Therefore the coefficient-finding frontier is now:
\[
d_+(p),\qquad d_-(p),\qquad m(p)
\]
for the non-enriched same-shell block.

\section{1. Exact \(m=1\) block}

Let the minimal same-shell non-enriched basis be
\[
\mathcal B_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}
=
\{|G_+,\eta\rangle,\ |G_-,\eta\rangle\},
\]
where \(\eta\) is one internal state orthogonal to the enriched shell doublet.

Then the projected block is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
H_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}(p)
=
\begin{pmatrix}
d_+(p) & m(p)\\
\overline{m(p)} & d_-(p)
\end{pmatrix},
}
\label{eq:m1_block_final}
\end{equation}
with
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_\pm(p)
=
\langle G_\pm,\eta|H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(1)}(p)|G_\pm,\eta\rangle,
\qquad
m(p)
=
\langle G_+,\eta|H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(1)}(p)|G_-,\eta\rangle.
}
\label{eq:m1_entries_final}
\end{equation}

This is the exact finite matrix that must be computed in the current working branch. :contentReference[oaicite:2]{index=2}

\section{2. Exact eigenvalues}

Since the block is Hermitian, its eigenvalues are real and equal to
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\lambda_\pm(p)
=
\frac{d_+(p)+d_-(p)}{2}
\pm
\sqrt{
\left(\frac{d_+(p)-d_-(p)}{2}\right)^2+|m(p)|^2
}.
}
\label{eq:m1_eigs_final}
\end{equation}

Therefore the finite non-enriched benchmark is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
=
\inf_{|p|\le \rho}
\min\{|\lambda_+(p)|,|\lambda_-(p)|\}.
}
\label{eq:m1_gap_final}
\end{equation}
This is exactly the object that must be inserted into the master benchmark. 

\section{3. Exact zero-avoidance condition}

A zero eigenvalue occurs iff
\[
\det H_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}(p)=0.
\]
Since
\[
\det H_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}(p)=d_+(p)d_-(p)-|m(p)|^2,
\]
we get the exact condition
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
0\in \operatorname{spec}\bigl(H_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}(p)\bigr)
\iff
d_+(p)d_-(p)=|m(p)|^2.
}
\label{eq:m1_zero_exact}
\end{equation}

Hence the same-shell non-enriched sector is spectrally separated from zero on \(|p|\le \rho\) if
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+(p)d_-(p)-|m(p)|^2\neq 0
\qquad
\forall |p|\le \rho.
}
\label{eq:m1_zero_avoid}
\end{equation}

\section{4. Useful lower bounds}

\subsection{4.1 Symmetric-sign regime}

Suppose
\[
d_+(p),\ d_-(p)
\]
have the same sign on \(|p|\le \rho\).
Then
\[
\min\{|\lambda_+(p)|,|\lambda_-(p)|\}
=
\frac{|d_+(p)+d_-(p)|}{2}
-
\sqrt{
\left(\frac{d_+(p)-d_-(p)}{2}\right)^2+|m(p)|^2
}.
\]
So an explicit sufficient lower bound is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
\ge
\inf_{|p|\le \rho}
\left[
\frac{|d_+(p)+d_-(p)|}{2}
-
\sqrt{
\left(\frac{d_+(p)-d_-(p)}{2}\right)^2+|m(p)|^2
}
\right].
}
\label{eq:m1_gap_lb_general}
\end{equation}

\subsection{4.2 Nearly symmetric diagonal case}

If
\[
d_+(p)=d(p)+\delta d(p),
\qquad
d_-(p)=d(p)-\delta d(p),
\]
then
\[
\lambda_\pm(p)=d(p)\pm \sqrt{\delta d(p)^2+|m(p)|^2},
\]
and therefore
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\min\{|\lambda_+(p)|,|\lambda_-(p)|\}
=
\left|
\,|d(p)|-\sqrt{\delta d(p)^2+|m(p)|^2}\,
\right|.
}
\label{eq:m1_gap_symmetric}
\end{equation}

Hence a very useful sufficient condition is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|d(p)|>\sqrt{\delta d(p)^2+|m(p)|^2}
\qquad
\forall |p|\le \rho,
}
\label{eq:m1_gap_simple_suff}
\end{equation}
which implies
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
\ge
\inf_{|p|\le \rho}
\left(
|d(p)|-\sqrt{\delta d(p)^2+|m(p)|^2}
\right)>0.
}
\label{eq:m1_gap_simple_lb}
\end{equation}

\subsection{4.3 Equal-diagonal subcase}

If, in addition,
\[
d_+(p)=d_-(p)=d(p),
\]
then
\[
\lambda_\pm(p)=d(p)\pm |m(p)|,
\]
so the exact gap becomes
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
=
\inf_{|p|\le \rho}
\bigl||d(p)|-|m(p)|\bigr|.
}
\label{eq:m1_gap_equaldiag}
\end{equation}
Thus zero is avoided iff
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|d(p)|\neq |m(p)|
\qquad
\forall |p|\le \rho.
}
\label{eq:m1_equaldiag_zeroavoid}
\end{equation}

\section{5. Truncation-to-exact usable benchmark}

The exact same-shell non-enriched benchmark is obtained from the finite truncation by
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}
\ge
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
-
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}.
}
\label{eq:m1_upgrade}
\end{equation}
Hence the usable benchmark entry is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
-
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}.
}
\label{eq:m1_usable_entry}
\end{equation}
If
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
<
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)},
}
\label{eq:m1_positive_cond}
\end{equation}
then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}>0.
}
\label{eq:m1_positive_exact}
\end{equation}
This is the exact finite-to-exact upgrade theorem specialized to \(m=1\). 

\section{6. Insertion into the explicit branch benchmark}

For the explicit canonical branch
\[
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \gamma_E=1,\qquad \gamma_O=0,
\]
the full benchmark side becomes
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{bench},\rho}^{\mathrm{fin}}
=
\min\Biggl\{
4K-|r_*|,
\;
\sqrt{M_\sigma^2+c_\sigma^2(q_*-\rho)^2},
\;
q_*^2\left|
(\lambda+\mu)+\frac{g^2}{M_\sigma^2+c_\sigma^2q_*^2}
\right|,
\;
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
-
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
\Biggr\}.
}
\label{eq:m1_branch_bench}
\end{equation}

The branch-inserted Step-IV gate is therefore the single finite inequality
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\min\Biggl\{
4K-|r_*|,
\;
\sqrt{M_\sigma^2+c_\sigma^2(q_*-\rho)^2},
\;
q_*^2\left|
(\lambda+\mu)+\frac{g^2}{M_\sigma^2+c_\sigma^2q_*^2}
\right|,
\;
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
-
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
\Biggr\}
>
\eta_{R,\rho}.
}
\label{eq:m1_branch_gate}
\end{equation}

\section{7. What must actually be computed}

Thus the remaining same-shell coefficient-finding problem is now reduced to the following finite data:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+(p),\qquad d_-(p),\qquad m(p),\qquad
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}.
}
\label{eq:m1_remaining_data}
\end{equation}

Once these are known, the same-shell non-enriched benchmark is explicit and Step IV is fully reduced to a concrete finite inequality.

\section{Final Summary}

The same-shell non-enriched sector in the minimal truncation \(m=1\) is already reduced to the explicit Hermitian block
\[
\boxed{
H_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}(p)
=
\begin{pmatrix}
d_+(p) & m(p)\\
\overline{m(p)} & d_-(p)
\end{pmatrix}.
}
\]

Its exact eigenvalues are
\[
\boxed{
\lambda_\pm(p)
=
\frac{d_+(p)+d_-(p)}{2}
\pm
\sqrt{
\left(\frac{d_+(p)-d_-(p)}{2}\right)^2+|m(p)|^2
}.
}
\]

Therefore the finite benchmark is
\[
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
=
\inf_{|p|\le \rho}
\min\{|\lambda_+(p)|,|\lambda_-(p)|\}.
}
\]

A zero eigenvalue occurs iff
\[
\boxed{
d_+(p)d_-(p)=|m(p)|^2.
}
\]

In the equal-diagonal subcase \(d_+=d_-=d\), the exact gap simplifies to
\[
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
=
\inf_{|p|\le \rho}\bigl||d(p)|-|m(p)|\bigr|.
}
\]

The usable benchmark entry is
\[
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
-
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)},
}
\]
and if
\[
\boxed{
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
<
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)},
}
\]
then the exact same-shell non-enriched sector is spectrally separated from zero.

Hence, for the explicit branch
\[
\boxed{
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \gamma_E=1,\qquad \gamma_O=0,
}
\]
the full Step-IV gate is now reduced to the single finite inequality
\[
\boxed{
\min\Biggl\{
4K-|r_*|,
\;
\sqrt{M_\sigma^2+c_\sigma^2(q_*-\rho)^2},
\;
q_*^2\left|
(\lambda+\mu)+\frac{g^2}{M_\sigma^2+c_\sigma^2q_*^2}
\right|,
\;
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
-
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
\Biggr\}
>
\eta_{R,\rho}.
}
\]

So the genuinely remaining same-shell coefficient-finding problem is the finite computation of
\[
\boxed{
d_+(p),\qquad d_-(p),\qquad m(p),\qquad
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}.
}
\]

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\section{Coefficient-Finding Continuation for the Minimal Same-Shell Non-Enriched Slot}

\section{Short explanation}

The same-shell non-enriched contribution is now reduced to an explicit \(2\times2\) Hermitian matrix problem.
Therefore the remaining Step-IV benchmark is no longer abstract.
It is a finite coefficient audit for
\[
d_+(p),\qquad d_-(p),\qquad m(p),
\]
or, equivalently, for their small-\(p\) coefficients
\[
d_+^{(0)},\qquad d_-^{(0)},\qquad m_0,\qquad a_{\pm,i},\qquad b_i.
\]

\section{1. Exact \(m=1\) same-shell block}

Choose the minimal same-shell non-enriched basis
\[
\mathcal B_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}
=
\{|G_+,\eta\rangle,\ |G_-,\eta\rangle\},
\]
where \(\eta\) is one internal state orthogonal to the enriched shell doublet.

Then the projected block is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
H_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}(p)
=
\begin{pmatrix}
d_+(p) & m(p)\\
\overline{m(p)} & d_-(p)
\end{pmatrix},
}
\label{eq:cf_m1_block}
\end{equation}
with
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_\pm(p)
=
\langle G_\pm,\eta|H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(1)}(p)|G_\pm,\eta\rangle,
\qquad
m(p)
=
\langle G_+,\eta|H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(1)}(p)|G_-,\eta\rangle.
}
\label{eq:cf_m1_entries}
\end{equation}

This is the exact finite matrix that must be inserted into the explicit branch benchmark.

\section{2. Exact eigenvalues and benchmark gap}

Since \eqref{eq:cf_m1_block} is Hermitian, its eigenvalues are real:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\lambda_\pm(p)
=
\frac{d_+(p)+d_-(p)}{2}
\pm
\sqrt{
\left(\frac{d_+(p)-d_-(p)}{2}\right)^2+|m(p)|^2
}.
}
\label{eq:cf_m1_eigs}
\end{equation}

Hence the exact same-shell non-enriched benchmark is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
=
\inf_{|p|\le \rho}
\min\{|\lambda_+(p)|,|\lambda_-(p)|\}.
}
\label{eq:cf_m1_gap}
\end{equation}

A zero eigenvalue occurs iff
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+(p)d_-(p)-|m(p)|^2=0.
}
\label{eq:cf_m1_zero}
\end{equation}

So the whole same-shell non-enriched remote-gap problem is already reduced to the finite scalar triplet
\[
(d_+(p),d_-(p),m(p)).
\]

\section{3. Coercive split and practical sufficient criterion}

For \(m=1\), introduce the exact coercive split
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
D_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}(p)
=
\begin{pmatrix}
d_+(p) & 0\\
0 & d_-(p)
\end{pmatrix},
\qquad
R_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}(p)
=
\begin{pmatrix}
0 & m(p)\\
\overline{m(p)} & 0
\end{pmatrix}.
}
\label{eq:cf_coercive_split}
\end{equation}
Then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
=
\inf_{|p|\le \rho}\min\{|d_+(p)|,|d_-(p)|\},
\qquad
\eta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
=
\sup_{|p|\le \rho}|m(p)|.
}
\label{eq:cf_delta_eta}
\end{equation}

Therefore the exact practical sufficient condition is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
>
\eta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
\Longrightarrow
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}>0.
}
\label{eq:cf_coercive_criterion}
\end{equation}

This is the same uniform Gershgorin/coercive criterion specialized to the minimal \(2\times2\) block.

\section{4. Small-\(p\) coefficient extraction}

Expand near \(p=0\):
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_\pm(p)=d_\pm^{(0)}+p_i a_{\pm,i}+O(|p|^2),
\qquad
m(p)=m_0+p_i b_i+O(|p|^2).
}
\label{eq:cf_smallp}
\end{equation}
Here
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_\pm^{(0)}
=
\langle G_\pm,\eta|H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(1)}(0)|G_\pm,\eta\rangle,
\qquad
m_0
=
\langle G_+,\eta|H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(1)}(0)|G_-,\eta\rangle,
}
\label{eq:cf_zero_coeffs}
\end{equation}
and
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
a_{\pm,i}
=
\left.
\partial_{p_i}
\langle G_\pm,\eta|H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(1)}(p)|G_\pm,\eta\rangle
\right|_{p=0},
\qquad
b_i
=
\left.
\partial_{p_i}
\langle G_+,\eta|H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(1)}(p)|G_-,\eta\rangle
\right|_{p=0}.
}
\label{eq:cf_linear_coeffs}
\end{equation}

Thus the same-shell coefficient-finding problem is now precisely the computation of the finite matrix elements
\[
d_+^{(0)},\qquad d_-^{(0)},\qquad m_0,\qquad a_{\pm,i},\qquad b_i.
\]

\section{5. Zero-momentum sufficient condition}

A sufficient condition for zero-momentum closure is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\min\{|d_+^{(0)}|,|d_-^{(0)}|\}>|m_0|.
}
\label{eq:cf_zero_suff}
\end{equation}

If, in addition, the linear correction satisfies
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\sup_{|p|\le \rho}
\max\{|p_i a_{+,i}|,\ |p_i a_{-,i}|,\ |p_i b_i|\}
\le \varepsilon_\rho
<
\min\{|d_+^{(0)}|,|d_-^{(0)}|\}-|m_0|,
}
\label{eq:cf_smallp_control}
\end{equation}
then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}>0.
}
\label{eq:cf_smallp_gap}
\end{equation}

So the practical benchmark is fully reduced to one zero-momentum inequality and one small-\(p\) perturbation budget.

\section{6. Equal-diagonal subcase}

If the explicit branch realization happens to satisfy
\[
d_+(p)=d_-(p)=d(p),
\]
then
\[
\lambda_\pm(p)=d(p)\pm |m(p)|.
\]
Hence the exact benchmark simplifies to
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
=
\inf_{|p|\le \rho}\bigl||d(p)|-|m(p)|\bigr|.
}
\label{eq:cf_equaldiag_gap}
\end{equation}
In particular, a sufficient zero-momentum condition becomes
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|d^{(0)}|>|m_0|.
}
\label{eq:cf_equaldiag_zero}
\end{equation}

This is the sharpest practical shortcut whenever the same-shell complementary state inherits a valley-symmetric diagonal entry from the shell Hamiltonian.

\section{7. Upgrade to the usable benchmark entry}

The exact usable entry in the final Step-IV benchmark is not just
\(\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}\), but
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
-
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}.
}
\label{eq:cf_usable_entry}
\end{equation}
If
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
<
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)},
}
\label{eq:cf_upgrade_positive}
\end{equation}
then the exact same-shell non-enriched sector remains spectrally separated from zero.

\section{8. Insertion into the explicit branch Step-IV gate}

For the explicit branch
\[
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \gamma_E=1,\qquad \gamma_O=0,
\]
the benchmark side becomes
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{bench},\rho}^{\mathrm{fin}}
=
\min\Biggl\{
4K-|r_*|,
\;
\sqrt{M_\sigma^2+c_\sigma^2(q_*-\rho)^2},
\;
q_*^2\left|
(\lambda+\mu)+\frac{g^2}{M_\sigma^2+c_\sigma^2q_*^2}
\right|,
\;
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
-
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
\Biggr\}.
}
\label{eq:cf_branch_bench}
\end{equation}

Thus the final remote-gap gate for this branch is the single explicit inequality
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\min\Biggl\{
4K-|r_*|,
\;
\sqrt{M_\sigma^2+c_\sigma^2(q_*-\rho)^2},
\;
q_*^2\left|
(\lambda+\mu)+\frac{g^2}{M_\sigma^2+c_\sigma^2q_*^2}
\right|,
\;
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
-
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
\Biggr\}
>
\eta_{R,\rho}.
}
\label{eq:cf_branch_gate}
\end{equation}

\section{9. Honest endpoint}

Therefore the genuinely remaining same-shell coefficient-finding problem is no longer conceptual.
It is the finite computation of
\[
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)},\qquad d_-^{(0)},\qquad m_0,\qquad a_{\pm,i},\qquad b_i,\qquad
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}.
}
\label{eq:cf_remaining}
\]
Once these are inserted, the same-shell non-enriched benchmark is fully explicit.

\section{Final Summary}

The same-shell non-enriched slot in the minimal truncation \(m=1\) is already reduced to the explicit Hermitian block
\[
\boxed{
H_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}(p)
=
\begin{pmatrix}
d_+(p) & m(p)\\
\overline{m(p)} & d_-(p)
\end{pmatrix}.
}
\]

Its exact eigenvalues are
\[
\boxed{
\lambda_\pm(p)
=
\frac{d_+(p)+d_-(p)}{2}
\pm
\sqrt{
\left(\frac{d_+(p)-d_-(p)}{2}\right)^2+|m(p)|^2
}.
}
\]

Hence the benchmark is
\[
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
=
\inf_{|p|\le \rho}\min\{|\lambda_+(p)|,|\lambda_-(p)|\}.
}
\]

A practical sufficient route is the coercive split
\[
\boxed{
\delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
=
\inf_{|p|\le \rho}\min\{|d_+(p)|,|d_-(p)|\},
\qquad
\eta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
=
\sup_{|p|\le \rho}|m(p)|,
}
\]
together with
\[
\boxed{
\delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
>
\eta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
\Longrightarrow
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}>0.
}
\]

Near \(p=0\),
\[
\boxed{
d_\pm(p)=d_\pm^{(0)}+p_i a_{\pm,i}+O(|p|^2),
\qquad
m(p)=m_0+p_i b_i+O(|p|^2),
}
\]
so the same-shell coefficient-finding problem reduces to the finite data
\[
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)},\qquad d_-^{(0)},\qquad m_0,\qquad a_{\pm,i},\qquad b_i.
}
\]

A sufficient zero-momentum condition is
\[
\boxed{
\min\{|d_+^{(0)}|,|d_-^{(0)}|\}>|m_0|.
}
\]
If, moreover, the small-\(p\) perturbation budget is controlled, then
\[
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}>0.
}
\]

Therefore, for the explicit branch
\[
\boxed{
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \gamma_E=1,\qquad \gamma_O=0,
}
\]
the final Step-IV gate is reduced to
\[
\boxed{
\min\Biggl\{
4K-|r_*|,
\;
\sqrt{M_\sigma^2+c_\sigma^2(q_*-\rho)^2},
\;
q_*^2\left|
(\lambda+\mu)+\frac{g^2}{M_\sigma^2+c_\sigma^2q_*^2}
\right|,
\;
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}-\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
\Biggr\}
>
\eta_{R,\rho}.
}
\]

So the genuinely remaining same-shell benchmark work is the explicit computation of
\[
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)},\ d_-^{(0)},\ m_0,\ a_{\pm,i},\ b_i,\ 
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}.
}
\]

\section{Actual Operator Decomposition of \texorpdfstring{$d_\pm^{(0)}$}{dpm0} and \texorpdfstring{$m_0$}{m0} in the Minimal Same-Shell Non-Enriched Slot}

\section{Short explanation}

The same-shell non-enriched \(m=1\) benchmark is already reduced to the \(2\times2\) Hermitian block
\[
H_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}(p)
=
\begin{pmatrix}
d_+(p) & m(p)\\
\overline{m(p)} & d_-(p)
\end{pmatrix}.
\]
What remains is to write the coefficients
\[
d_+^{(0)},\qquad d_-^{(0)},\qquad m_0
\]
directly in terms of the actual shell-projected Bloch operator.

The correct decomposition is:
\[
\text{reference/direct same-shell block}
\quad+\quad
\text{second-order heavy Schur correction}.
\]

\section{1. Minimal same-shell non-enriched basis}

Let
\[
H_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)
=
\Pi_{S_*}\,H_{\mathrm{eff}}(k_*+p)\,\Pi_{S_*}
\]
be the shell-projected operator near the folded Bragg point.
Choose the minimal same-shell complementary basis
\[
\mathcal B_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}
=
\{|+\rangle,\ |-\rangle\},
\qquad
|+\rangle:=|G_+,\eta\rangle,
\qquad
|-\rangle:=|G_-,\eta\rangle,
\]
where \(\eta\) is one internal state orthogonal to the enriched shell doublet.

Then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
H_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}(p)
=
\begin{pmatrix}
d_+(p) & m(p)\\
\overline{m(p)} & d_-(p)
\end{pmatrix},
}
\label{eq:op_m1_block}
\end{equation}
with
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_\pm(p)=\langle \pm|H_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)|\pm\rangle,
\qquad
m(p)=\langle +|H_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)|-\rangle.
}
\label{eq:op_m1_entries}
\end{equation}

\section{2. Reference + perturbation split}

Write the shell operator as
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
H_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)
=
H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(0)}(p)+V_{\mathrm{shell}}(p),
}
\label{eq:op_split}
\end{equation}
where \(H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(0)}(p)\) is the reference shell operator and \(V_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)\) collects the explicit shell perturbations induced by the refined/Class-II branch.

At \(p=0\), define the direct same-shell matrix elements
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
D_+^{(0)}
:=
\langle +|H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(0)}(0)|+\rangle,
\qquad
D_-^{(0)}
:=
\langle -|H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(0)}(0)|-\rangle,
}
\label{eq:op_ref_diag}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
M^{(0)}
:=
\langle +|H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(0)}(0)|-\rangle.
}
\label{eq:op_ref_offdiag}
\end{equation}
Likewise for the explicit shell perturbation,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
V_{++}
:=
\langle +|V_{\mathrm{shell}}(0)|+\rangle,
\qquad
V_{--}
:=
\langle -|V_{\mathrm{shell}}(0)|-\rangle,
}
\label{eq:op_Vdiag}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
V_{+-}
:=
\langle +|V_{\mathrm{shell}}(0)|-\rangle.
}
\label{eq:op_Voffdiag}
\end{equation}

If one stopped at the direct shell level, one would simply have
\[
d_+^{(0)}=D_+^{(0)}+V_{++},
\qquad
d_-^{(0)}=D_-^{(0)}+V_{--},
\qquad
m_0=M^{(0)}+V_{+-}.
\]

\section{3. Heavy-state second-order correction}

Now include the heavy sector through the exact second-order Schur formula.
Choose a heavy basis \(\chi_\alpha\) diagonalizing the reference heavy block:
\[
\mathbb O^{(0)}\chi_\alpha=E_\alpha\chi_\alpha,
\qquad
E_\alpha\ge \Delta_H>0.
\]
Then the second-order correction to the low shell block is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
(\mathcal Y_{\mathrm{eff}}^{(2)})_{ab}
=
-\sum_\alpha
\frac{
K_{a\alpha}\,\overline{K_{b\alpha}}
}{E_\alpha},
}
\label{eq:op_second_order}
\end{equation}
where
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
K_{a\alpha}
=
\langle a|V_{\mathrm{shell}}(0)|\chi_\alpha\rangle,
\qquad
a\in\{+,-\}.
}
\label{eq:op_Kdef}
\end{equation}

Thus, in the present \(m=1\) same-shell complementary slot, the heavy-corrected coefficients are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
D_+^{(0)}+V_{++}
-
\sum_\alpha\frac{|K_{+\alpha}|^2}{E_\alpha},
}
\label{eq:op_dplus_final}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_-^{(0)}
=
D_-^{(0)}+V_{--}
-
\sum_\alpha\frac{|K_{-\alpha}|^2}{E_\alpha},
}
\label{eq:op_dminus_final}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_0
=
M^{(0)}+V_{+-}
-
\sum_\alpha\frac{K_{+\alpha}\,\overline{K_{-\alpha}}}{E_\alpha}.
}
\label{eq:op_m0_final}
\end{equation}

These are the actual finite operator formulas that must be evaluated.

\section{4. Useful symmetry reductions}

\subsection{4.1 Valley-symmetric reference block}

If the reference shell background is valley-symmetric in the complementary state,
\[
D_+^{(0)}=D_-^{(0)}=:D^{(0)},
\]
then the diagonal asymmetry comes only from the explicit shell perturbation and/or the heavy Schur correction:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}-d_-^{(0)}
=
(V_{++}-V_{--})
-
\sum_\alpha
\frac{|K_{+\alpha}|^2-|K_{-\alpha}|^2}{E_\alpha}.
}
\label{eq:op_diag_asym}
\end{equation}

\subsection{4.2 Equal-diagonal subcase}

If moreover
\[
V_{++}=V_{--},
\qquad
|K_{+\alpha}|=|K_{-\alpha}|
\ \ \forall\alpha,
\]
then
\[
d_+^{(0)}=d_-^{(0)}=:d^{(0)},
\]
and the exact zero-momentum gap reduces to
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},0}^{(1)}
=
\bigl||d^{(0)}|-|m_0|\bigr|.
}
\label{eq:op_equaldiag_gap}
\end{equation}

In that subcase, a sufficient nonzero benchmark condition is simply
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|d^{(0)}|>|m_0|.
}
\label{eq:op_equaldiag_suff}
\end{equation}

\section{5. Small-\(p\) coefficients}

The linear coefficients are obtained by differentiating the same matrix elements:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
a_{+,i}
=
\left.\partial_{p_i}d_+(p)\right|_{p=0},
\qquad
a_{-,i}
=
\left.\partial_{p_i}d_-(p)\right|_{p=0},
\qquad
b_i
=
\left.\partial_{p_i}m(p)\right|_{p=0}.
}
\label{eq:op_linear_defs}
\end{equation}

Using the same decomposition,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
a_{+,i}
=
\partial_{p_i}\langle +|H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(0)}(p)+V_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)|+\rangle\big|_{0}
-
\partial_{p_i}
\sum_\alpha
\frac{|K_{+\alpha}(p)|^2}{E_\alpha(p)}
\Big|_{0},
}
\label{eq:op_aplus}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
a_{-,i}
=
\partial_{p_i}\langle -|H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(0)}(p)+V_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)|-\rangle\big|_{0}
-
\partial_{p_i}
\sum_\alpha
\frac{|K_{-\alpha}(p)|^2}{E_\alpha(p)}
\Big|_{0},
}
\label{eq:op_aminus}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
b_i
=
\partial_{p_i}\langle +|H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(0)}(p)+V_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)|-\rangle\big|_{0}
-
\partial_{p_i}
\sum_\alpha
\frac{K_{+\alpha}(p)\,\overline{K_{-\alpha}(p)}}{E_\alpha(p)}
\Big|_{0}.
}
\label{eq:op_bi}
\end{equation}

Thus all small-\(p\) data are again reduced to finite matrix elements and heavy-state sums.

\section{6. Zero-momentum practical sufficient criterion}

The zero-momentum sufficient criterion becomes
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\min\{|d_+^{(0)}|,|d_-^{(0)}|\}>|m_0|,
}
\label{eq:op_zero_suff}
\end{equation}
with \(d_\pm^{(0)}\) and \(m_0\) given explicitly by
\eqref{eq:op_dplus_final}--\eqref{eq:op_m0_final}.

If moreover the small-\(p\) correction budget satisfies
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\sup_{|p|\le \rho}
\max\{|p_i a_{+,i}|,\ |p_i a_{-,i}|,\ |p_i b_i|\}
<
\min\{|d_+^{(0)}|,|d_-^{(0)}|\}-|m_0|,
}
\label{eq:op_smallp_suff}
\end{equation}
then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}>0.
}
\label{eq:op_gap_positive}
\end{equation}

\section{7. Insertion into the explicit branch remote benchmark}

For the explicit canonical branch
\[
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \gamma_E=1,\qquad \gamma_O=0,
\]
the full Step-IV benchmark remains
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{bench},\rho}^{\mathrm{fin}}
=
\min\Biggl\{
4K-|r_*|,
\;
\sqrt{M_\sigma^2+c_\sigma^2(q_*-\rho)^2},
\;
q_*^2\left|
(\lambda+\mu)+\frac{g^2}{M_\sigma^2+c_\sigma^2q_*^2}
\right|,
\;
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
-
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
\Biggr\}.
}
\label{eq:op_branch_bench}
\end{equation}

Hence the genuinely remaining same-shell coefficient-finding problem is the finite evaluation of
\[
\boxed{
D_\pm^{(0)},\ V_{++},\ V_{--},\ V_{+-},\ K_{+\alpha},\ K_{-\alpha},\ E_\alpha,
\quad
\text{and the corresponding derivatives at }p=0.
}
\label{eq:op_remaining_data}
\]

\section{Final Summary}

For the minimal same-shell non-enriched complementary slot \(m=1\), the exact block is
\[
\boxed{
H_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}(p)
=
\begin{pmatrix}
d_+(p) & m(p)\\
\overline{m(p)} & d_-(p)
\end{pmatrix}.
}
\]

The actual zero-momentum coefficients are not abstract anymore.
They are given by the direct same-shell matrix elements plus the heavy-state second-order Schur correction:
\[
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
D_+^{(0)}+V_{++}
-
\sum_\alpha\frac{|K_{+\alpha}|^2}{E_\alpha},
}
\]
\[
\boxed{
d_-^{(0)}
=
D_-^{(0)}+V_{--}
-
\sum_\alpha\frac{|K_{-\alpha}|^2}{E_\alpha},
}
\]
\[
\boxed{
m_0
=
M^{(0)}+V_{+-}
-
\sum_\alpha\frac{K_{+\alpha}\,\overline{K_{-\alpha}}}{E_\alpha}.
}
\]

Therefore the same-shell coefficient-finding problem is reduced to the finite matrix-element data
\[
\boxed{
D_\pm^{(0)},\ V_{++},\ V_{--},\ V_{+-},\ K_{+\alpha},\ K_{-\alpha},\ E_\alpha.
}
\]

The practical zero-momentum sufficient condition is
\[
\boxed{
\min\{|d_+^{(0)}|,|d_-^{(0)}|\}>|m_0|.
}
\]

If, in addition, the linear small-\(p\) budget is controlled via
\[
a_{\pm,i}=\partial_{p_i}d_\pm(0),\qquad
b_i=\partial_{p_i}m(0),
\]
then
\[
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}>0.
}
\]

Thus, for the explicit branch
\[
\boxed{
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \gamma_E=1,\qquad \gamma_O=0,
}
\]
the final Step-IV benchmark is reduced to a completely finite Hermitian matrix computation. The only remaining work is the literal evaluation of these matrix elements in the chosen shell-projected Bloch basis.

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\section{Canonical Minimal Choice \texorpdfstring{$\eta=z_0$}{eta=z0} and Explicit \(m=1\) Same-Shell Non-Enriched Coefficients}

\section{Short explanation}

The minimal same-shell non-enriched basis was previously left abstract as
\[
\mathcal B_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}
=
\{|G_+,\eta\rangle,\ |G_-,\eta\rangle\},
\]
with \(\eta\) any internal state orthogonal to the enriched shell doublet.

In the canonical locked basis
\[
(z_0,u_1,u_2),
\]
the enriched shell carrier uses the tangent doublet \((u_1,u_2)\).
Therefore the natural minimal complementary same-shell state is the locked line itself:
\[
\boxed{
\eta=z_0.
}
\]

This makes the same-shell non-enriched \(m=1\) sector fully explicit.

\section{1. Canonical minimal same-shell non-enriched basis}

Fix the canonical locked basis
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
z_0=(1,0,0)^T,
\qquad
u_1=(0,1,0)^T,
\qquad
u_2=(0,0,1)^T.
}
\label{eq:eta_can_basis}
\end{equation}

The enriched shell carrier occupies
\[
\mathcal H_D
=
\mathrm{span}\{|G_+,u_1\rangle,\ |G_+,u_2\rangle,\ |G_-,u_1\rangle,\ |G_-,u_2\rangle\}.
\]
Hence the minimal same-shell complementary state is chosen as
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\eta=z_0.
}
\label{eq:eta_choice}
\end{equation}

Therefore the minimal same-shell non-enriched basis becomes
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|+\rangle:=|G_+,z_0\rangle,
\qquad
|-\rangle:=|G_-,z_0\rangle.
}
\label{eq:eta_basis_pm}
\end{equation}

In this basis the projected same-shell non-enriched block is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
H_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}(p)
=
\begin{pmatrix}
d_+(p) & m(p)\\
\overline{m(p)} & d_-(p)
\end{pmatrix},
}
\label{eq:eta_m1_block}
\end{equation}
with
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_\pm(p)=\langle \pm|H_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)|\pm\rangle,
\qquad
m(p)=\langle +|H_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)|-\rangle.
}
\label{eq:eta_entries}
\end{equation}

\section{2. Exact direct-plus-heavy decomposition}

The effective shell operator is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
H_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)
=
\Pi_{S_*}\,H_{\mathrm{eff}}(k_*+p)\,\Pi_{S_*},
\qquad
H_{\mathrm{eff}}(k)
=
H_{\Psi\Psi}(k)-H_{\Psi X}(k)H_{XX}(k)^{-1}H_{X\Psi}(k).
}
\label{eq:eta_Heff}
\end{equation}

Hence the zero-momentum coefficients split exactly as
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
L_{++}^{(z_0)}
-
\Sigma_{++}^{(z_0)},
}
\label{eq:eta_dplus}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_-^{(0)}
=
L_{--}^{(z_0)}
-
\Sigma_{--}^{(z_0)},
}
\label{eq:eta_dminus}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_0
=
L_{+-}^{(z_0)}
-
\Sigma_{+-}^{(z_0)},
}
\label{eq:eta_m0}
\end{equation}
where
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
L_{ab}^{(z_0)}
:=
\langle a|H_{\Psi\Psi}(k_*)|b\rangle,
\qquad
a,b\in\{+,-\},
}
\label{eq:eta_Lab}
\end{equation}
and
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Sigma_{ab}^{(z_0)}
:=
\langle a|H_{\Psi X}(k_*)H_{XX}(k_*)^{-1}H_{X\Psi}(k_*)|b\rangle.
}
\label{eq:eta_Sigmaab}
\end{equation}

\section{3. Heavy-eigenbasis form of the Schur term}

Choose a heavy basis \(\chi_\alpha\) diagonalizing the reference heavy block:
\[
\mathbb O^{(0)}\chi_\alpha=E_\alpha\chi_\alpha,
\qquad
E_\alpha\ge \Delta_H>0.
\]
Then the exact second-order formula is
\[
(\mathcal Y_{\mathrm{eff}}^{(2)})_{ab}
=
-
\sum_\alpha
\frac{K_{a\alpha}\overline{K_{b\alpha}}}{E_\alpha}.
\]
Therefore the same-shell complementary Schur entries are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Sigma_{++}^{(z_0)}
=
\sum_\alpha
\frac{|K_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2}{E_\alpha},
\qquad
\Sigma_{--}^{(z_0)}
=
\sum_\alpha
\frac{|K_{-\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2}{E_\alpha},
}
\label{eq:eta_Sigmad}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Sigma_{+-}^{(z_0)}
=
\sum_\alpha
\frac{K_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}\overline{K_{-\alpha}^{(z_0)}}}{E_\alpha},
}
\label{eq:eta_Sigmaoff}
\end{equation}
with
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
K_{\pm\alpha}^{(z_0)}
=
\langle G_\pm,z_0|V_{\mathrm{shell}}(0)|\chi_\alpha\rangle.
}
\label{eq:eta_Kpm}
\end{equation}
Thus
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
L_{++}^{(z_0)}
-
\sum_\alpha\frac{|K_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2}{E_\alpha},
}
\label{eq:eta_dplus_final}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_-^{(0)}
=
L_{--}^{(z_0)}
-
\sum_\alpha\frac{|K_{-\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2}{E_\alpha},
}
\label{eq:eta_dminus_final}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_0
=
L_{+-}^{(z_0)}
-
\sum_\alpha\frac{K_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}\overline{K_{-\alpha}^{(z_0)}}}{E_\alpha}.
}
\label{eq:eta_m0_final}
\end{equation}

\section{4. Direct shell matrix elements in Bloch form}

Because the projected shell operator is built from the Bloch kernel at the folded Bragg point,
the direct terms are simply
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
L_{++}^{(z_0)}
=
\langle G_+,z_0|H_{\Psi\Psi}(k_*)|G_+,z_0\rangle,
}
\label{eq:eta_Lpp}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
L_{--}^{(z_0)}
=
\langle G_-,z_0|H_{\Psi\Psi}(k_*)|G_-,z_0\rangle,
}
\label{eq:eta_Lmm}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
L_{+-}^{(z_0)}
=
\langle G_+,z_0|H_{\Psi\Psi}(k_*)|G_-,z_0\rangle.
}
\label{eq:eta_Lpm}
\end{equation}

If one writes the direct shell block on the \(z_0\)-line as
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0,\pm}(0):=\langle G_\pm,z_0|H_{\Psi\Psi}(k_*)|G_\pm,z_0\rangle,
\qquad
B_{z_0}(0):=\langle G_+,z_0|H_{\Psi\Psi}(k_*)|G_-,z_0\rangle,
}
\label{eq:eta_EBz0}
\end{equation}
then the actual coefficients are simply
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}=E_{z_0,+}(0)-\Sigma_{++}^{(z_0)},
\qquad
d_-^{(0)}=E_{z_0,-}(0)-\Sigma_{--}^{(z_0)},
\qquad
m_0=B_{z_0}(0)-\Sigma_{+-}^{(z_0)}.
}
\label{eq:eta_finalcompact}
\end{equation}

\section{5. Valley-symmetric reference subcase}

If the direct shell background is valley-symmetric on the locked line, i.e.
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0,+}(0)=E_{z_0,-}(0)=:E_{z_0}^{(0)},
}
\label{eq:eta_valley_sym}
\end{equation}
then the diagonal asymmetry is entirely Schur-generated:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}-d_-^{(0)}
=
-
\sum_\alpha
\frac{|K_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2-|K_{-\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2}{E_\alpha}.
}
\label{eq:eta_diag_asym}
\end{equation}

If, further, the heavy couplings are valley-symmetric in norm,
\[
|K_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}|=|K_{-\alpha}^{(z_0)}|
\quad\forall \alpha,
\]
then
\[
d_+^{(0)}=d_-^{(0)}=:d^{(0)},
\]
and the zero-momentum eigenvalues reduce to
\[
\lambda_\pm(0)=d^{(0)}\pm |m_0|.
\]
Hence the exact zero-momentum non-enriched gap becomes
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},0}^{(1)}
=
\bigl||d^{(0)}|-|m_0|\bigr|.
}
\label{eq:eta_zero_gap}
\end{equation}
Therefore a sufficient zero-momentum condition is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|d^{(0)}|>|m_0|.
}
\label{eq:eta_zero_suff}
\end{equation}

\section{6. Small-\(p\) coefficients}

The linear coefficients are obtained by differentiating the same matrix elements:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
a_{+,i}
=
\left.\partial_{p_i}
\langle G_+,z_0|H_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)|G_+,z_0\rangle
\right|_{p=0},
}
\label{eq:eta_aplus}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
a_{-,i}
=
\left.\partial_{p_i}
\langle G_-,z_0|H_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)|G_-,z_0\rangle
\right|_{p=0},
}
\label{eq:eta_aminus}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
b_i
=
\left.\partial_{p_i}
\langle G_+,z_0|H_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)|G_-,z_0\rangle
\right|_{p=0}.
}
\label{eq:eta_bi}
\end{equation}

If these derivatives satisfy the small-\(p\) budget
\[
\sup_{|p|\le \rho}
\max\{|p_i a_{+,i}|,\ |p_i a_{-,i}|,\ |p_i b_i|\}
<
\min\{|d_+^{(0)}|,|d_-^{(0)}|\}-|m_0|,
\]
then
\[
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}>0.
\]

\section{7. Insertion into the explicit branch Step-IV gate}

For the explicit branch
\[
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \gamma_E=1,\qquad \gamma_O=0,
\]
the benchmark-side last slot is exactly
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
-
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)},
}
\label{eq:eta_usable}
\end{equation}
with \(\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}\) determined by
\eqref{eq:eta_dplus_final}--\eqref{eq:eta_m0_final}.

Hence the genuinely remaining same-shell coefficient-finding data are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0,+}(0),\quad
E_{z_0,-}(0),\quad
B_{z_0}(0),\quad
K_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)},\quad
K_{-\alpha}^{(z_0)},\quad
E_\alpha,
}
\label{eq:eta_remaining}
\end{equation}
together with the small-\(p\) derivatives \(a_{\pm,i},b_i\).

\section{Final Summary}

The minimal same-shell non-enriched complementary state can be fixed canonically as
\[
\boxed{
\eta=z_0,
}
\]
where
\[
(z_0,u_1,u_2)
\]
is the canonical locked internal basis and \((u_1,u_2)\) span the enriched shell doublet.

Hence the minimal same-shell non-enriched basis is
\[
\boxed{
|+\rangle=|G_+,z_0\rangle,
\qquad
|-\rangle=|G_-,z_0\rangle.
}
\]

The exact zero-momentum coefficients of the \(m=1\) non-enriched block are then
\[
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0,+}(0)
-
\sum_\alpha\frac{|K_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2}{E_\alpha},
}
\]
\[
\boxed{
d_-^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0,-}(0)
-
\sum_\alpha\frac{|K_{-\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2}{E_\alpha},
}
\]
\[
\boxed{
m_0
=
B_{z_0}(0)
-
\sum_\alpha\frac{K_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}\overline{K_{-\alpha}^{(z_0)}}}{E_\alpha}.
}
\]

Thus the same-shell coefficient-finding problem is reduced to the finite matrix-element data
\[
\boxed{
E_{z_0,+}(0),\quad
E_{z_0,-}(0),\quad
B_{z_0}(0),\quad
K_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)},\quad
K_{-\alpha}^{(z_0)},\quad
E_\alpha.
}
\]

If the direct shell background is valley-symmetric and the heavy-coupling norms are also valley-symmetric, then
\[
d_+^{(0)}=d_-^{(0)}=:d^{(0)},
\]
and the zero-momentum gap simplifies to
\[
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},0}^{(1)}
=
\bigl||d^{(0)}|-|m_0|\bigr|.
}
\]
A sufficient zero-momentum condition is then
\[
\boxed{
|d^{(0)}|>|m_0|.
}
\]

Therefore, for the explicit branch
\[
\boxed{
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \gamma_E=1,\qquad \gamma_O=0,
}
\]
the final same-shell benchmark slot has been reduced to a completely finite matrix-element audit on the canonical locked-line complementary state.

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\section{Canonical Complement \texorpdfstring{$\eta=z_0$}{eta=z0} and Actual Extraction of \texorpdfstring{$d_\pm^{(0)}$}{dpm0}, \texorpdfstring{$m_0$}{m0}}

\section{Short explanation}

The minimal same-shell non-enriched benchmark is already reduced to the Hermitian block
\[
H_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}(p)
=
\begin{pmatrix}
d_+(p) & m(p)\\
\overline{m(p)} & d_-(p)
\end{pmatrix},
\]
with
\[
d_\pm(p)=\langle G_\pm,\eta|H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(1)}(p)|G_\pm,\eta\rangle,
\qquad
m(p)=\langle G_+,\eta|H_{\mathrm{shell}}^{(1)}(p)|G_-,\eta\rangle.
\]

To make this fully concrete, we now fix the minimal canonical complement
\[
\eta=z_0.
\]
This turns the final same-shell benchmark slot into a literal \(2\times2\) matrix-element computation on the locked line.

\section{1. Canonical minimal same-shell complement}

Fix the canonical locked basis
\[
z_0=e_1,
\qquad
u_1=e_2,
\qquad
u_2=e_3.
\]
The enriched shell carrier occupies the tangent doublet
\[
\mathrm{span}\{|G_\pm,u_1\rangle,\ |G_\pm,u_2\rangle\},
\]
so the minimal same-shell non-enriched complement is naturally
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\eta=z_0.
}
\label{eq:z0_choice}
\end{equation}

Hence the \(m=1\) same-shell non-enriched basis is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|+\rangle:=|G_+,z_0\rangle,
\qquad
|-\rangle:=|G_-,z_0\rangle.
}
\label{eq:z0_basis}
\end{equation}

\section{2. Exact direct-plus-Schur decomposition}

The shell operator is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
H_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)
=
\Pi_{S_*}H_{\mathrm{eff}}(k_*+p)\Pi_{S_*},
\qquad
H_{\mathrm{eff}}(k)
=
H_{\Psi\Psi}(k)-H_{\Psi X}(k)H_{XX}(k)^{-1}H_{X\Psi}(k).
}
\label{eq:z0_Heff}
\end{equation}

Therefore the zero-momentum coefficients split exactly as
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0,+}(0)-\Sigma_{++}^{(z_0)},
\qquad
d_-^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0,-}(0)-\Sigma_{--}^{(z_0)},
\qquad
m_0
=
B_{z_0}(0)-\Sigma_{+-}^{(z_0)},
}
\label{eq:z0_direct_schur}
\end{equation}
where
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0,+}(0):=\langle G_+,z_0|H_{\Psi\Psi}(k_*)|G_+,z_0\rangle,
}
\label{eq:z0_Eplus}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0,-}(0):=\langle G_-,z_0|H_{\Psi\Psi}(k_*)|G_-,z_0\rangle,
}
\label{eq:z0_Eminus}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
B_{z_0}(0):=\langle G_+,z_0|H_{\Psi\Psi}(k_*)|G_-,z_0\rangle,
}
\label{eq:z0_B}
\end{equation}
and
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Sigma_{ab}^{(z_0)}
=
\langle a|H_{\Psi X}(k_*)H_{XX}(k_*)^{-1}H_{X\Psi}(k_*)|b\rangle,
\qquad
a,b\in\{+,-\}.
}
\label{eq:z0_Sigma}
\end{equation}

In the heavy eigenbasis \(\chi_\alpha\),
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Sigma_{ab}^{(z_0)}
=
\sum_\alpha
\frac{K_{a\alpha}^{(z_0)}\overline{K_{b\alpha}^{(z_0)}}}{E_\alpha},
\qquad
K_{\pm\alpha}^{(z_0)}:=\langle G_\pm,z_0|V_{\mathrm{shell}}(0)|\chi_\alpha\rangle.
}
\label{eq:z0_heavy_sum}
\end{equation}

\section{3. Actual \(T_\star=T^1\) calculation on the \(z_0\)-line}

Now specialize to the explicit branch
\[
T_\star=T^1.
\]
In the canonical basis,
\[
T^1=\frac12
\begin{pmatrix}
0&1&0\\
1&0&0\\
0&0&0
\end{pmatrix},
\qquad
z_0=e_1.
\]
Hence
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
z_0^\dagger T^1 z_0=0.
}
\label{eq:z0_T1_diagzero}
\end{equation}

The explicit \(J\)-harmonic coefficient is
\[
\mathsf J_{i,r}^{a}(G_*;q)
=
i\,q_i\,A_{G_*}\,u_r^\dagger T^a z_0
+
i\,(G_*)_i\,A_{G_*}\,z_0^\dagger T^a u_r.
\]
Setting
\[
u_r=z_0,
\qquad
a=1,
\]
and using \eqref{eq:z0_T1_diagzero}, both terms vanish:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathsf J_{i,0}^{1}(G_*;q)=0.
}
\label{eq:z0_Jzero}
\end{equation}

Therefore the \(JJ\)-part of the Schur correction vanishes identically on the minimal same-shell complementary \(z_0\)-slot:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Sigma_{ab}^{(JJ;z_0)}=0,
\qquad
a,b\in\{+,-\}.
}
\label{eq:z0_JJzero}
\end{equation}

\section{4. Exact reduced formulas after the \(JJ\)-vanishing}

Hence the actual coefficients reduce to
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0,+}(0)-\Sigma_{++}^{(JK+KK;z_0)},
}
\label{eq:z0_dplus_reduced}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_-^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0,-}(0)-\Sigma_{--}^{(JK+KK;z_0)},
}
\label{eq:z0_dminus_reduced}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_0
=
B_{z_0}(0)-\Sigma_{+-}^{(JK+KK;z_0)}.
}
\label{eq:z0_m0_reduced}
\end{equation}

If one performs the pure-\(J\) subaudit, i.e. temporarily switches off the \(K\)-sector contribution in the same-shell complementary slot, then the formulas collapse further to
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}=E_{z_0,+}(0),
\qquad
d_-^{(0)}=E_{z_0,-}(0),
\qquad
m_0=B_{z_0}(0).
}
\label{eq:z0_pureJ}
\end{equation}

\section{5. Direct core interpretation}

The shell documents already imply that constant Bragg pair-mixing is controlled by the primitive \(Q=G_*\) Fourier coefficient of the effective shell potential,
\[
M_0=\widehat U_{\mathrm{eff}}(G_*)\,\mathbf 1_2,
\]
while longitudinal slope has a direct periodic core contribution.
Therefore the direct same-shell complementary opposite-valley entry \(B_{z_0}(0)\) is the locked-line analogue of this primitive first-shell Bragg coefficient.

Thus the direct zero-momentum same-shell benchmark is controlled by:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0,+}(0),\qquad E_{z_0,-}(0),\qquad B_{z_0}(0),
}
\label{eq:z0_direct_triplet}
\end{equation}
with the mediated correction only entering through the \(JK/KK\) part.

\section{6. Practical zero-momentum sufficient condition}

The same-shell zero-momentum sufficient condition becomes
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\min\{|d_+^{(0)}|,|d_-^{(0)}|\}>|m_0|.
}
\label{eq:z0_zero_suff}
\end{equation}

If the \(JK/KK\) correction is subleading or absent in the chosen minimal branch realization, this reduces to the explicit direct condition
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\min\{|E_{z_0,+}(0)|,|E_{z_0,-}(0)|\}>|B_{z_0}(0)|.
}
\label{eq:z0_direct_suff}
\end{equation}

If moreover the direct shell background is valley-symmetric on the locked line,
\[
E_{z_0,+}(0)=E_{z_0,-}(0)=:E_{z_0}^{(0)},
\]
then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|E_{z_0}^{(0)}|>|B_{z_0}(0)|
\Longrightarrow
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},0}^{(1)}>0.
}
\label{eq:z0_equaldiag_suff}
\end{equation}

\section{7. Final same-shell benchmark insertion}

Therefore, for the explicit branch
\[
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \gamma_E=1,\qquad \gamma_O=0,
\]
the genuinely remaining same-shell benchmark data are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0,+}(0),\quad
E_{z_0,-}(0),\quad
B_{z_0}(0),\quad
\Sigma_{++}^{(JK+KK;z_0)},\quad
\Sigma_{--}^{(JK+KK;z_0)},\quad
\Sigma_{+-}^{(JK+KK;z_0)},
}
\label{eq:z0_remaining}
\end{equation}
together with the small-\(p\) derivatives.
The \(JJ\)-part is already zero by the explicit \(T^1\) canonical computation.

\section{Final Summary}

With the canonical locked internal basis
\[
(z_0,u_1,u_2)=(e_1,e_2,e_3),
\]
the minimal same-shell non-enriched complementary state can be fixed as
\[
\boxed{
\eta=z_0.
}
\]

Hence the \(m=1\) same-shell non-enriched basis is
\[
\boxed{
|+\rangle=|G_+,z_0\rangle,
\qquad
|-\rangle=|G_-,z_0\rangle.
}
\]

The zero-momentum coefficients are exactly
\[
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0,+}(0)-\Sigma_{++}^{(z_0)},
\qquad
d_-^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0,-}(0)-\Sigma_{--}^{(z_0)},
\qquad
m_0
=
B_{z_0}(0)-\Sigma_{+-}^{(z_0)}.
}
\]

For the explicit branch
\[
\boxed{
T_\star=T^1,
}
\]
one has
\[
z_0^\dagger T^1 z_0=0,
\]
and therefore the \(J\)-harmonic coefficient on the \(z_0\)-line vanishes:
\[
\boxed{
\mathsf J_{i,0}^{1}(G_*;q)=0.
}
\]
Consequently,
\[
\boxed{
\Sigma_{ab}^{(JJ;z_0)}=0.
}
\]

Hence the actual same-shell benchmark coefficients reduce to
\[
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0,+}(0)-\Sigma_{++}^{(JK+KK;z_0)},
}
\]
\[
\boxed{
d_-^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0,-}(0)-\Sigma_{--}^{(JK+KK;z_0)},
}
\]
\[
\boxed{
m_0
=
B_{z_0}(0)-\Sigma_{+-}^{(JK+KK;z_0)}.
}
\]

In the pure-\(J\) subaudit this collapses further to
\[
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}=E_{z_0,+}(0),
\qquad
d_-^{(0)}=E_{z_0,-}(0),
\qquad
m_0=B_{z_0}(0).
}
\]

Therefore the zero-momentum same-shell sufficient condition becomes
\[
\boxed{
\min\{|d_+^{(0)}|,|d_-^{(0)}|\}>|m_0|.
}
\]
If the \(JK/KK\) correction is subleading or absent, this simplifies to
\[
\boxed{
\min\{|E_{z_0,+}(0)|,|E_{z_0,-}(0)|\}>|B_{z_0}(0)|.
}
\]

So the genuinely remaining benchmark-side data for this explicit branch are
\[
\boxed{
E_{z_0,+}(0),\quad
E_{z_0,-}(0),\quad
B_{z_0}(0),\quad
\Sigma_{++}^{(JK+KK;z_0)},\quad
\Sigma_{--}^{(JK+KK;z_0)},\quad
\Sigma_{+-}^{(JK+KK;z_0)}.
}
\]
The \(JJ\)-part is already computed and vanishes exactly.

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\section{Direct Locked-Core Evaluation of \texorpdfstring{$d_\pm^{(0)}$}{dpm0} and \texorpdfstring{$m_0$}{m0} on the Canonical Complement \texorpdfstring{$\eta=z_0$}{eta=z0}}

\section{Short explanation}

We now stop leaving the same-shell non-enriched direct part abstract.

Fix the canonical complementary state
\[
\eta=z_0.
\]
Then the minimal same-shell non-enriched basis is
\[
|+\rangle=|G_+,z_0\rangle,
\qquad
|-\rangle=|G_-,z_0\rangle.
\]

The direct zero-momentum coefficients come from the shell-projected triplet block \(H_{\Psi\Psi}(k_*)\),
while the mediator only enters through the Schur correction.
For the explicit branch \(T_\star=T^1\), the \(JJ\)-part vanishes exactly on the \(z_0\)-line,
so the remaining same-shell benchmark data reduce to:
\[
\text{direct locked-core block}
\quad+\quad
JK/KK\text{-residual Schur correction}.
\]

\section{1. Minimal \(m=1\) same-shell complementary block}

With the canonical choice
\[
\eta=z_0,
\]
define
\[
|+\rangle:=|G_+,z_0\rangle,
\qquad
|-\rangle:=|G_-,z_0\rangle.
\]
Then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
H_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}(p)
=
\begin{pmatrix}
d_+(p) & m(p)\\
\overline{m(p)} & d_-(p)
\end{pmatrix},
}
\label{eq:dir_m1_block}
\end{equation}
where
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_\pm(p)=\langle G_\pm,z_0|H_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)|G_\pm,z_0\rangle,
\qquad
m(p)=\langle G_+,z_0|H_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)|G_-,z_0\rangle.
}
\label{eq:dir_entries}
\end{equation}

At \(p=0\),
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}=E_{z_0,+}(0)-\Sigma_{++}^{(z_0)},
\qquad
d_-^{(0)}=E_{z_0,-}(0)-\Sigma_{--}^{(z_0)},
\qquad
m_0=B_{z_0}(0)-\Sigma_{+-}^{(z_0)}.
}
\label{eq:dir_direct_schur}
\end{equation}

\section{2. Direct shell block on the \(z_0\)-line}

The direct triplet Bloch block has the standard periodic-core form
\[
H_{\Psi\Psi}(k)=H_0(k)+U^{(\mathrm{per})}+U^{(\mathrm{lock})}.
\]
Therefore the direct same-shell complementary matrix elements are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0,+}(0)
=
\langle G_+,z_0|H_0(k_*)|G_+,z_0\rangle
+
\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{per})}(0)+U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(0)\bigr]_{z_0z_0},
}
\label{eq:dir_Eplus_general}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0,-}(0)
=
\langle G_-,z_0|H_0(k_*)|G_-,z_0\rangle
+
\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{per})}(0)+U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(0)\bigr]_{z_0z_0},
}
\label{eq:dir_Eminus_general}
\end{equation}
and the opposite-valley direct Bragg entry is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
B_{z_0}(0)
=
\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{per})}(G_*)+U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(G_*)\bigr]_{z_0z_0}.
}
\label{eq:dir_B_general}
\end{equation}

Because \(|G_+|=|G_-|=|k_*|=q_*/2\), the direct diagonal symbol is valley-symmetric:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\langle G_+,z_0|H_0(k_*)|G_+,z_0\rangle
=
\langle G_-,z_0|H_0(k_*)|G_-,z_0\rangle
=:h_{z_0}(k_*).
}
\label{eq:dir_hsym}
\end{equation}

Hence
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0,+}(0)=E_{z_0,-}(0)=:E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0),
}
\label{eq:dir_Eeq}
\end{equation}
with
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
=
h_{z_0}(k_*)
+
\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{per})}(0)+U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(0)\bigr]_{z_0z_0}.
}
\label{eq:dir_Ez0}
\end{equation}

\section{3. Explicit scalar safe-sector evaluation}

Inside the current safe scalar sector, the only periodic scalar contribution is
\[
U_{\mathrm{per}}^{\mathrm{tot}}(x)=u|\phi_0(x)|^2,
\]
and its first-shell Fourier coefficient is
\[
\widehat U_{\mathrm{per}}^{\mathrm{tot}}(Q)=4uA^2
\qquad
(Q\in S_{\mathrm{BCC}}).
\]
Therefore the direct opposite-valley locked-line Bragg entry is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
B_{z_0}^{\mathrm{scalar}}(0)=4uA^2.
}
\label{eq:dir_Bscalar}
\end{equation}

For the diagonal zero-mode coefficient, in the same Fourier normalization one has
\[
\widehat{|\phi_0|^2}(0)=12A^2,
\]
because only the \(Q_1=Q_2\) pairs contribute at zero momentum and the first shell has 12 elements.
Hence the direct diagonal scalar shift is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\bigl[U_{\mathrm{per}}^{\mathrm{tot}}(0)\bigr]_{z_0z_0}=12uA^2.
}
\label{eq:dir_Uscalar0}
\end{equation}

Thus, in the scalar-only locked core,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)=h_{z_0}(k_*)+12uA^2+\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(0)\bigr]_{z_0z_0},
}
\label{eq:dir_Escalar}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
B_{z_0}(0)=4uA^2+\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(G_*)\bigr]_{z_0z_0}.
}
\label{eq:dir_Bscalarlock}
\end{equation}

If no additional direct locked-line scalar refinement is switched on, this collapses to
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)=h_{z_0}(k_*)+12uA^2,
\qquad
B_{z_0}(0)=4uA^2.
}
\label{eq:dir_EB_minimal}
\end{equation}

\section{4. Actual \(T_\star=T^1\) branch: \(JJ\)-part vanishes}

Now specialize to the explicit branch
\[
T_\star=T^1,
\qquad
z_0=e_1.
\]
Then
\[
T^1=\frac12
\begin{pmatrix}
0&1&0\\
1&0&0\\
0&0&0
\end{pmatrix},
\qquad
z_0^\dagger T^1 z_0=0.
\]
Therefore the \(z_0\)-line \(J\)-harmonic coefficient vanishes:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathsf J_{i,0}^{1}(G_*;q)=0.
}
\label{eq:dir_Jzero}
\end{equation}
Hence the \(JJ\)-part of the Schur correction is exactly absent:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Sigma_{ab}^{(JJ;z_0)}=0,
\qquad a,b\in\{+,-\}.
}
\label{eq:dir_JJzero}
\end{equation}

So the actual same-shell coefficients reduce to
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)-\Sigma_{++}^{(JK+KK;z_0)},
}
\label{eq:dir_dplus}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_-^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)-\Sigma_{--}^{(JK+KK;z_0)},
}
\label{eq:dir_dminus}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_0
=
B_{z_0}(0)-\Sigma_{+-}^{(JK+KK;z_0)}.
}
\label{eq:dir_m0}
\end{equation}

\section{5. Pure-\(J\) subaudit}

If one performs the pure-\(J\) subaudit, i.e. temporarily suppresses the \(K\)-sector residual in the same-shell complementary slot, then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}=d_-^{(0)}=E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0),
\qquad
m_0=B_{z_0}(0).
}
\label{eq:dir_pureJ}
\end{equation}

In the minimal scalar-only locked core this gives
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}=d_-^{(0)}=h_{z_0}(k_*)+12uA^2,
\qquad
m_0=4uA^2.
}
\label{eq:dir_minimal_numbers}
\end{equation}

Hence the zero-momentum eigenvalues are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\lambda_\pm(0)=h_{z_0}(k_*)+12uA^2\pm 4uA^2.
}
\label{eq:dir_zeroeig}
\end{equation}
That is,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\lambda_+(0)=h_{z_0}(k_*)+16uA^2,
\qquad
\lambda_-(0)=h_{z_0}(k_*)+8uA^2.
}
\label{eq:dir_zeroeig_explicit}
\end{equation}

Therefore the exact zero-momentum same-shell non-enriched gap in this minimal subaudit is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},0}^{(1)}
=
\min\bigl\{|h_{z_0}(k_*)+16uA^2|,\ |h_{z_0}(k_*)+8uA^2|\bigr\}.
}
\label{eq:dir_gap0}
\end{equation}

A sufficient condition is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
h_{z_0}(k_*)>-8uA^2.
}
\label{eq:dir_suff}
\end{equation}
In particular, if
\[
u>0,\qquad h_{z_0}(k_*)\ge 0,
\]
then
\[
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},0}^{(1)}>0
\]
automatically.

\section{6. Honest endpoint}

Thus the direct part of the same-shell benchmark is now explicit.

For the branch
\[
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \eta=z_0,
\]
the \(JJ\)-Schur part vanishes exactly, and the remaining same-shell benchmark data are reduced to:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
h_{z_0}(k_*),\qquad
uA^2,\qquad
\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(0)\bigr]_{z_0z_0},\qquad
\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(G_*)\bigr]_{z_0z_0},\qquad
\Sigma_{ab}^{(JK+KK;z_0)}.
}
\label{eq:dir_remaining}
\end{equation}
So the direct locked-core part is finished; only the \(JK/KK\) residual remains.

\section{Final Summary}

For the minimal same-shell non-enriched complementary choice
\[
\boxed{
\eta=z_0,
}
\]
the exact zero-momentum coefficients are
\[
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}=E_{z_0,+}(0)-\Sigma_{++}^{(z_0)},
\qquad
d_-^{(0)}=E_{z_0,-}(0)-\Sigma_{--}^{(z_0)},
\qquad
m_0=B_{z_0}(0)-\Sigma_{+-}^{(z_0)}.
}
\]

For the explicit branch
\[
\boxed{
T_\star=T^1,
}
\]
one has
\[
\boxed{
z_0^\dagger T^1 z_0=0,
\qquad
\mathsf J_{i,0}^{1}(G_*;q)=0,
\qquad
\Sigma_{ab}^{(JJ;z_0)}=0.
}
\]

Hence the actual same-shell benchmark coefficients reduce to
\[
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)-\Sigma_{++}^{(JK+KK;z_0)},
\qquad
d_-^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)-\Sigma_{--}^{(JK+KK;z_0)},
}
\]
\[
\boxed{
m_0
=
B_{z_0}(0)-\Sigma_{+-}^{(JK+KK;z_0)}.
}
\]

In the pure-\(J\) subaudit this simplifies further to
\[
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}=d_-^{(0)}=E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0),
\qquad
m_0=B_{z_0}(0).
}
\]

Inside the minimal scalar-only locked core,
\[
\boxed{
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)=h_{z_0}(k_*)+12uA^2,
\qquad
B_{z_0}(0)=4uA^2.
}
\]

Therefore the zero-momentum eigenvalues are
\[
\boxed{
\lambda_+(0)=h_{z_0}(k_*)+16uA^2,
\qquad
\lambda_-(0)=h_{z_0}(k_*)+8uA^2.
}
\]

So the exact zero-momentum same-shell non-enriched gap in this minimal subaudit is
\[
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},0}^{(1)}
=
\min\bigl\{|h_{z_0}(k_*)+16uA^2|,\ |h_{z_0}(k_*)+8uA^2|\bigr\}.
}
\]

Thus the direct locked-core part of the same-shell benchmark is finished.
The only remaining benchmark-side residual is the finite \(JK/KK\)-Schur correction
\[
\boxed{
\Sigma_{ab}^{(JK+KK;z_0)}.
}
\]

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\section{Further Reduction of the Canonical Same-Shell Benchmark: Only the \(KK\) Residual Survives on \texorpdfstring{$\eta=z_0$}{eta=z0}}

\section{Short explanation}

We continue the actual coefficient extraction for the minimal same-shell non-enriched slot
\[
|+\rangle=|G_+,z_0\rangle,
\qquad
|-\rangle=|G_-,z_0\rangle
\]
inside the explicit branch
\[
T_\star=T^1.
\]

The key observation is that the \(z_0\)-line has no \(J\)-harmonic coupling in this branch.
Therefore, in the Schur correction
\[
-\frac1{M_X^2}(\alpha_XJ+\beta_XK)(\alpha_XJ+\beta_XK)^\dagger,
\]
both the \(JJ\) and \(JK\) pieces vanish on the same-shell complementary \(z_0\)-slot.
Only the \(KK\) piece survives.

Thus the last benchmark-side same-shell coefficients reduce to:
\[
\text{direct locked-core block}
\quad+\quad
\text{pure }KK\text{ heavy residual}.
\]

\section{1. Minimal canonical same-shell non-enriched block}

Fix the canonical locked basis
\[
z_0=e_1,\qquad u_1=e_2,\qquad u_2=e_3,
\]
and the minimal same-shell complementary basis
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|+\rangle:=|G_+,z_0\rangle,
\qquad
|-\rangle:=|G_-,z_0\rangle.
}
\label{eq:kk_basis}
\end{equation}

Then the \(m=1\) same-shell non-enriched block is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
H_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr}}^{(1)}(p)
=
\begin{pmatrix}
d_+(p) & m(p)\\
\overline{m(p)} & d_-(p)
\end{pmatrix},
}
\label{eq:kk_block}
\end{equation}
with
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_\pm(p)=\langle G_\pm,z_0|H_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)|G_\pm,z_0\rangle,
\qquad
m(p)=\langle G_+,z_0|H_{\mathrm{shell}}(p)|G_-,z_0\rangle.
}
\label{eq:kk_entries}
\end{equation}

At \(p=0\),
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}=E_{z_0,+}(0)-\Sigma_{++}^{(z_0)},
\qquad
d_-^{(0)}=E_{z_0,-}(0)-\Sigma_{--}^{(z_0)},
\qquad
m_0=B_{z_0}(0)-\Sigma_{+-}^{(z_0)}.
}
\label{eq:kk_direct_schur}
\end{equation}

\section{2. Full Schur structure and vanishing of the \(J\)-external couplings}

The effective shell operator is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
H_{\mathrm{eff}}(k)
=
H_{\Psi\Psi}(k)
-
\frac{1}{M_X^2}
(\alpha_X\mathcal J(k)+\beta_X\mathcal K(k))
(\alpha_X\mathcal J(k)+\beta_X\mathcal K(k))^\dagger.
}
\label{eq:kk_Heff}
\end{equation}
Hence the same-shell complementary Schur term is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Sigma_{ab}^{(z_0)}
=
\frac{1}{M_X^2}
\Bigl\langle a\Big|
(\alpha_X\mathcal J+\beta_X\mathcal K)
(\alpha_X\mathcal J+\beta_X\mathcal K)^\dagger
\Big|b\Bigr\rangle,
\qquad
a,b\in\{+,-\}.
}
\label{eq:kk_Sigma_full}
\end{equation}

Now specialize to
\[
T_\star=T^1.
\]
In the canonical basis,
\[
T^1=\frac12
\begin{pmatrix}
0&1&0\\
1&0&0\\
0&0&0
\end{pmatrix},
\qquad
z_0=e_1,
\]
so
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
z_0^\dagger T^1 z_0=0.
}
\label{eq:kk_diagzero}
\end{equation}

Using the explicit shell harmonic \(J\)-coefficient
\[
\mathsf J_{i,r}^{a}(G_*;q)
=
i\,q_i\,A_{G_*}\,u_r^\dagger T^a z_0
+
i\,(G_*)_i\,A_{G_*}\,z_0^\dagger T^a u_r,
\]
and setting \(u_r=z_0,\ a=1\), one gets
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathsf J_{i,0}^{1}(G_*;q)=0.
}
\label{eq:kk_Jzero}
\end{equation}

Therefore the external \(z_0\)-line \(J\)-couplings vanish:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\langle G_\pm,z_0|\mathcal J(k_*)|\chi_\alpha\rangle=0
\qquad
\forall \alpha.
}
\label{eq:kk_Jextzero}
\end{equation}

\section{3. Consequence: \(JJ\) and \(JK\) both vanish on the \(z_0\)-slot}

Because the external \(z_0\)-line has no \(J\)-coupling, the Schur pieces satisfy
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Sigma_{ab}^{(JJ;z_0)}=0,
\qquad
\Sigma_{ab}^{(JK;z_0)}=0,
\qquad
a,b\in\{+,-\}.
}
\label{eq:kk_JJJK_zero}
\end{equation}

Hence only the \(KK\)-residual survives:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Sigma_{ab}^{(z_0)}=\Sigma_{ab}^{(KK;z_0)}.
}
\label{eq:kk_onlyKK}
\end{equation}

Thus the exact zero-momentum coefficients reduce to
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0,+}(0)-\Sigma_{++}^{(KK;z_0)},
}
\label{eq:kk_dplus}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_-^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0,-}(0)-\Sigma_{--}^{(KK;z_0)},
}
\label{eq:kk_dminus}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_0
=
B_{z_0}(0)-\Sigma_{+-}^{(KK;z_0)}.
}
\label{eq:kk_m0}
\end{equation}

\section{4. Direct locked-core part}

The direct triplet shell block along the locked line is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0,+}(0)
=
h_{z_0}(k_*)
+
\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{per})}(0)+U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(0)\bigr]_{z_0z_0},
}
\label{eq:kk_Eplus}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0,-}(0)
=
h_{z_0}(k_*)
+
\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{per})}(0)+U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(0)\bigr]_{z_0z_0},
}
\label{eq:kk_Eminus}
\end{equation}
and the opposite-valley direct Bragg entry is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
B_{z_0}(0)
=
\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{per})}(G_*)+U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(G_*)\bigr]_{z_0z_0}.
}
\label{eq:kk_B}
\end{equation}

Therefore the direct diagonal part is valley-symmetric:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0,+}(0)=E_{z_0,-}(0)=:E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0).
}
\label{eq:kk_evalley}
\end{equation}

Inside the minimal scalar-only locked core,
\[
U_{\mathrm{per}}^{\mathrm{tot}}(x)=u|\phi_0(x)|^2,
\qquad
\widehat U_{\mathrm{per}}^{\mathrm{tot}}(0)=12uA^2,
\qquad
\widehat U_{\mathrm{per}}^{\mathrm{tot}}(G_*)=4uA^2.
\]
Hence
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
=
\omega_B(k_*)+12uA^2+\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(0)\bigr]_{z_0z_0},
}
\label{eq:kk_Edir}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
B_{z_0}(0)
=
4uA^2+\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(G_*)\bigr]_{z_0z_0},
}
\label{eq:kk_Bdir}
\end{equation}
where
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\omega_B(k_*)
=
-\mu^2+Z|k_*|^2-Y|k_*|^4
=
-\mu^2+\frac{Zq_*^2}{4}-\frac{Yq_*^4}{16}.
}
\label{eq:kk_omega}
\end{equation}

If no additional direct locked-line refinement is switched on, this simplifies to
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)=\omega_B(k_*)+12uA^2,
\qquad
B_{z_0}(0)=4uA^2.
}
\label{eq:kk_EBminimal}
\end{equation}

\section{5. Pure-\(J\) subaudit as a strict lower-complexity benchmark}

If one temporarily suppresses the \(K\)-sector in the same-shell complementary slot, then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}=d_-^{(0)}=E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0),
\qquad
m_0=B_{z_0}(0).
}
\label{eq:kk_pureJ}
\end{equation}

In the minimal scalar-only locked core this yields
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}=d_-^{(0)}=\omega_B(k_*)+12uA^2,
\qquad
m_0=4uA^2.
}
\label{eq:kk_pureJ_minimal}
\end{equation}

Hence the zero-momentum eigenvalues are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\lambda_\pm(0)=\omega_B(k_*)+12uA^2\pm 4uA^2,
}
\label{eq:kk_pureJ_eigs}
\end{equation}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\lambda_+(0)=\omega_B(k_*)+16uA^2,
\qquad
\lambda_-(0)=\omega_B(k_*)+8uA^2.
}
\label{eq:kk_pureJ_eigs_explicit}
\end{equation}

Therefore the exact zero-momentum same-shell benchmark in this strict subaudit is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},0}^{(1)}
=
\min\bigl\{
|\omega_B(k_*)+16uA^2|,
\ |\omega_B(k_*)+8uA^2|
\bigr\}.
}
\label{eq:kk_gap0}
\end{equation}

A sufficient positivity condition is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\omega_B(k_*)>-8uA^2.
}
\label{eq:kk_gap_suff}
\end{equation}

\section{6. Final exact \(KK\)-residual form}

Choose a heavy basis \(\chi_\alpha\) diagonalizing the heavy block with eigenvalues \(E_\alpha>0\).
Since only the \(K\)-external couplings survive, define
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal K_{\pm\alpha}^{(z_0)}
:=
\langle G_\pm,z_0|\mathcal K(k_*)|\chi_\alpha\rangle.
}
\label{eq:kk_Kpm}
\end{equation}
Then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Sigma_{++}^{(KK;z_0)}
=
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
\sum_\alpha
\frac{|\mathcal K_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2}{E_\alpha},
}
\label{eq:kk_Spp}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Sigma_{--}^{(KK;z_0)}
=
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
\sum_\alpha
\frac{|\mathcal K_{-\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2}{E_\alpha},
}
\label{eq:kk_Smm}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Sigma_{+-}^{(KK;z_0)}
=
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
\sum_\alpha
\frac{\mathcal K_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}\overline{\mathcal K_{-\alpha}^{(z_0)}}}{E_\alpha}.
}
\label{eq:kk_Spm}
\end{equation}

So the actual same-shell coefficients are finally
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
\sum_\alpha
\frac{|\mathcal K_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2}{E_\alpha},
}
\label{eq:kk_dplus_final}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_-^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
\sum_\alpha
\frac{|\mathcal K_{-\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2}{E_\alpha},
}
\label{eq:kk_dminus_final}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_0
=
B_{z_0}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
\sum_\alpha
\frac{\mathcal K_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}\overline{\mathcal K_{-\alpha}^{(z_0)}}}{E_\alpha}.
}
\label{eq:kk_m0_final}
\end{equation}

Therefore the entire same-shell benchmark-side frontier for this explicit branch has been reduced to the finite \(KK\)-overlap sums.

\section{Final Summary}

For the explicit branch
\[
\boxed{
T_\star=T^1,
\qquad
\eta=z_0,
}
\]
the minimal same-shell non-enriched benchmark coefficients satisfy
\[
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}=E_{z_0,+}(0)-\Sigma_{++}^{(z_0)},
\qquad
d_-^{(0)}=E_{z_0,-}(0)-\Sigma_{--}^{(z_0)},
\qquad
m_0=B_{z_0}(0)-\Sigma_{+-}^{(z_0)}.
}
\]

Because
\[
z_0^\dagger T^1 z_0=0,
\]
the external \(z_0\)-line has no \(J\)-harmonic coupling. Therefore
\[
\boxed{
\Sigma^{(JJ;z_0)}=0,
\qquad
\Sigma^{(JK;z_0)}=0,
}
\]
and only the \(KK\)-residual survives:
\[
\boxed{
\Sigma^{(z_0)}=\Sigma^{(KK;z_0)}.
}
\]

The direct locked-core part is
\[
\boxed{
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
=
\omega_B(k_*)+12uA^2+[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(0)]_{z_0z_0},
}
\]
\[
\boxed{
B_{z_0}(0)
=
4uA^2+[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(G_*)]_{z_0z_0},
}
\]
with
\[
\boxed{
\omega_B(k_*)
=
-\mu^2+\frac{Zq_*^2}{4}-\frac{Yq_*^4}{16}.
}
\]

Hence the actual same-shell benchmark coefficients reduce to
\[
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
\sum_\alpha\frac{|\mathcal K_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2}{E_\alpha},
}
\]
\[
\boxed{
d_-^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
\sum_\alpha\frac{|\mathcal K_{-\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2}{E_\alpha},
}
\]
\[
\boxed{
m_0
=
B_{z_0}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
\sum_\alpha\frac{\mathcal K_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}\overline{\mathcal K_{-\alpha}^{(z_0)}}}{E_\alpha}.
}
\]

Thus the direct part of the same-shell benchmark is finished, and the genuinely remaining benchmark-side residual is the finite pure-\(KK\) overlap sum.

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\section{Pure \(KK\) Reduction of the Same-Shell Complementary Residual on \(\eta=z_0\)}

\section{Short explanation}

For the explicit branch
\[
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \eta=z_0,
\]
the same-shell non-enriched zero-momentum coefficients were reduced to
\[
d_+^{(0)}=E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)-\Sigma_{++}^{(KK;z_0)},
\qquad
d_-^{(0)}=E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)-\Sigma_{--}^{(KK;z_0)},
\qquad
m_0=B_{z_0}(0)-\Sigma_{+-}^{(KK;z_0)}.
\]

We now evaluate the surviving \(KK\)-piece at the level of explicit shell Fourier overlaps.
This turns the last same-shell benchmark residual into a finite quadratic form in the two transverse seed amplitudes
\[
\Lambda_E^{(0)},\qquad \Lambda_O^{(0)}.
\]

\section{1. Defect-background \(K\)-sector}

The minimal complete \(K\)-current is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
K_i^a[P,\psi]
=
\Tr(T^a\partial_iP)\,
\Bigl(
\Lambda_E^{(0)}E_j{}^{b}
+
\Lambda_O^{(0)}J_j{}^{b}
\Bigr)
D_j\psi_b.
}
\label{eq:KK_K_general}
\end{equation}

On the defect background,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\partial_iP_B
=
\delta_{i\xi}\,\theta'(\xi)\,(e_1z_B^\dagger+z_Be_1^\dagger),
}
\label{eq:KK_dPB}
\end{equation}
hence
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Tr(T^a\partial_iP_B)
=
\delta_{i\xi}\,\theta'(\xi)\,k_a(\theta),
}
\label{eq:KK_ka}
\end{equation}
and therefore
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
K_i^a[P_B,\psi]
=
\delta_{i\xi}\,\theta'(\xi)\,k_a(\theta)\,
\Bigl(
\Lambda_E^{(0)}E_j{}^b
+
\Lambda_O^{(0)}J_j{}^b
\Bigr)
D_j\psi_b.
}
\label{eq:KK_K_defect}
\end{equation}

This means that the surviving same-shell complementary couplings are already linear in
\[
\Lambda_E^{(0)},\qquad \Lambda_O^{(0)}.
\]

\section{2. Heavy-overlap amplitudes}

Let \(\chi_\alpha\) be the heavy eigenbasis with
\[
\mathbb O^{(0)}\chi_\alpha=E_\alpha\chi_\alpha,
\qquad
E_\alpha>0.
\]
Define the \(E\)-type and \(O\)-type same-shell complementary overlaps on the \(z_0\)-line by
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal E_{\pm\alpha}^{(z_0)}
:=
\left\langle
G_\pm,z_0
\middle|
\theta'(\xi)\,k_a(\theta)\,E_j{}^b D_j\psi_b
\middle|
\chi_\alpha
\right\rangle,
}
\label{eq:KK_Eoverlap}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal O_{\pm\alpha}^{(z_0)}
:=
\left\langle
G_\pm,z_0
\middle|
\theta'(\xi)\,k_a(\theta)\,J_j{}^b D_j\psi_b
\middle|
\chi_\alpha
\right\rangle.
}
\label{eq:KK_Ooverlap}
\end{equation}

Then the full \(K\)-overlap amplitudes factor as
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal K_{\pm\alpha}^{(z_0)}
=
\Lambda_E^{(0)}\,\mathcal E_{\pm\alpha}^{(z_0)}
+
\Lambda_O^{(0)}\,\mathcal O_{\pm\alpha}^{(z_0)}.
}
\label{eq:KK_factorized_overlap}
\end{equation}

Thus the same-shell complementary residual is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Sigma_{ab}^{(KK;z_0)}
=
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
\sum_\alpha
\frac{
\mathcal K_{a\alpha}^{(z_0)}
\overline{\mathcal K_{b\alpha}^{(z_0)}}
}{E_\alpha},
\qquad
a,b\in\{+,-\}.
}
\label{eq:KK_Sigma_general}
\end{equation}

\section{3. Explicit quadratic-form reduction}

Substituting \eqref{eq:KK_factorized_overlap} into \eqref{eq:KK_Sigma_general}, one gets
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Sigma_{ab}^{(KK;z_0)}
=
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
\Bigl[
(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\,\mathcal S_{ab}^{EE}
+
\Lambda_E^{(0)}\Lambda_O^{(0)}\,\mathcal S_{ab}^{EO}
+
(\Lambda_O^{(0)})^2\,\mathcal S_{ab}^{OO}
\Bigr],
}
\label{eq:KK_quadratic}
\end{equation}
where the finite overlap sums are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{ab}^{EE}
:=
\sum_\alpha
\frac{
\mathcal E_{a\alpha}^{(z_0)}
\overline{\mathcal E_{b\alpha}^{(z_0)}}
}{E_\alpha},
}
\label{eq:KK_SEE}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{ab}^{EO}
:=
\sum_\alpha
\frac{
\mathcal E_{a\alpha}^{(z_0)}
\overline{\mathcal O_{b\alpha}^{(z_0)}}
+
\mathcal O_{a\alpha}^{(z_0)}
\overline{\mathcal E_{b\alpha}^{(z_0)}}
}{E_\alpha},
}
\label{eq:KK_SEO}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{ab}^{OO}
:=
\sum_\alpha
\frac{
\mathcal O_{a\alpha}^{(z_0)}
\overline{\mathcal O_{b\alpha}^{(z_0)}}
}{E_\alpha}.
}
\label{eq:KK_SOO}
\end{equation}

Therefore the actual same-shell coefficients are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
\Bigl[
(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\,\mathcal S_{++}^{EE}
+
\Lambda_E^{(0)}\Lambda_O^{(0)}\,\mathcal S_{++}^{EO}
+
(\Lambda_O^{(0)})^2\,\mathcal S_{++}^{OO}
\Bigr],
}
\label{eq:KK_dplus_quad}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_-^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
\Bigl[
(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\,\mathcal S_{--}^{EE}
+
\Lambda_E^{(0)}\Lambda_O^{(0)}\,\mathcal S_{--}^{EO}
+
(\Lambda_O^{(0)})^2\,\mathcal S_{--}^{OO}
\Bigr],
}
\label{eq:KK_dminus_quad}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_0
=
B_{z_0}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
\Bigl[
(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\,\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}
+
\Lambda_E^{(0)}\Lambda_O^{(0)}\,\mathcal S_{+-}^{EO}
+
(\Lambda_O^{(0)})^2\,\mathcal S_{+-}^{OO}
\Bigr].
}
\label{eq:KK_m0_quad}
\end{equation}

\section{4. Pure-\(E\) residual subbranch}

If the same-shell complementary residual is evaluated in the pure-even subbranch
\[
\boxed{
\Lambda_O^{(0)}=0,
}
\]
then the formulas collapse to
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\,\mathcal S_{++}^{EE},
}
\label{eq:KK_dplus_Eonly}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_-^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\,\mathcal S_{--}^{EE},
}
\label{eq:KK_dminus_Eonly}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_0
=
B_{z_0}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\,\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}.
}
\label{eq:KK_m0_Eonly}
\end{equation}

This is the cleanest same-shell benchmark realization compatible with the explicit pure-\(E\) carrier branch.

\section{5. Positivity and Cauchy-type control}

For the diagonal entries one has manifest positivity:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{++}^{EE}\ge 0,\qquad
\mathcal S_{--}^{EE}\ge 0,
\qquad
\mathcal S_{++}^{OO}\ge 0,\qquad
\mathcal S_{--}^{OO}\ge 0.
}
\label{eq:KK_diag_positive}
\end{equation}
Moreover, by Cauchy--Schwarz,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}|^2
\le
\mathcal S_{++}^{EE}\,\mathcal S_{--}^{EE},
\qquad
|\mathcal S_{+-}^{OO}|^2
\le
\mathcal S_{++}^{OO}\,\mathcal S_{--}^{OO}.
}
\label{eq:KK_CS}
\end{equation}

Thus the off-diagonal same-shell residual cannot exceed the geometric mean of the two diagonal residual budgets.

\section{6. Practical zero-momentum sufficient condition}

The exact zero-momentum same-shell sufficient condition remains
\[
\min\{|d_+^{(0)}|,|d_-^{(0)}|\}>|m_0|.
\]
In the pure-even residual subbranch \(\Lambda_O^{(0)}=0\), this becomes
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\min\left\{
\left|
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{++}^{EE}
\right|,
\;
\left|
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{--}^{EE}
\right|
\right\}
>
\left|
B_{z_0}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}
\right|.
}
\label{eq:KK_zero_suff}
\end{equation}

If, in addition, valley symmetry holds on the residual norms,
\[
\mathcal S_{++}^{EE}=\mathcal S_{--}^{EE}=: \mathcal S_{\rm diag}^{EE},
\]
then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\left|
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{\rm diag}^{EE}
\right|
>
\left|
B_{z_0}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}
\right|
}
\label{eq:KK_zero_suff_sym}
\end{equation}
is sufficient.

\section{7. Final reduction of the same-shell benchmark}

Therefore, for the explicit branch
\[
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \eta=z_0,
\]
the same-shell benchmark side is fully reduced to the finite overlap data
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0),\qquad
B_{z_0}(0),\qquad
\mathcal S_{ab}^{EE},\qquad
\mathcal S_{ab}^{EO},\qquad
\mathcal S_{ab}^{OO},
}
\label{eq:KK_final_data}
\end{equation}
or, in the explicit pure-even residual subbranch,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0),\qquad
B_{z_0}(0),\qquad
\mathcal S_{++}^{EE},\qquad
\mathcal S_{--}^{EE},\qquad
\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}.
}
\label{eq:KK_final_data_Eonly}
\end{equation}

This is the literal finite coefficient set that remains to be inserted into the Step-IV same-shell benchmark.

\section{Final Summary}

For the explicit branch
\[
\boxed{
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \eta=z_0,
}
\]
the same-shell non-enriched benchmark residual is purely \(KK\):
\[
\boxed{
\Sigma^{(z_0)}=\Sigma^{(KK;z_0)}.
}
\]

Using the explicit defect-background \(K\)-ansatz,
\[
\boxed{
K_i^a[P_B,\psi]
=
\delta_{i\xi}\theta'(\xi)k_a(\theta)
\Bigl(
\Lambda_E^{(0)}E_j{}^b+\Lambda_O^{(0)}J_j{}^b
\Bigr)D_j\psi_b,
}
\]
the heavy overlap amplitudes factorize as
\[
\boxed{
\mathcal K_{\pm\alpha}^{(z_0)}
=
\Lambda_E^{(0)}\mathcal E_{\pm\alpha}^{(z_0)}
+
\Lambda_O^{(0)}\mathcal O_{\pm\alpha}^{(z_0)}.
}
\]

Therefore the same-shell residual is the quadratic form
\[
\boxed{
\Sigma_{ab}^{(KK;z_0)}
=
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
\Bigl[
(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{ab}^{EE}
+
\Lambda_E^{(0)}\Lambda_O^{(0)}\mathcal S_{ab}^{EO}
+
(\Lambda_O^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{ab}^{OO}
\Bigr],
}
\]
with finite overlap sums
\[
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{ab}^{EE},\qquad
\mathcal S_{ab}^{EO},\qquad
\mathcal S_{ab}^{OO}.
}
\]

Hence the actual zero-momentum same-shell coefficients are
\[
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)-\Sigma_{++}^{(KK;z_0)},
\qquad
d_-^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)-\Sigma_{--}^{(KK;z_0)},
}
\]
\[
\boxed{
m_0
=
B_{z_0}(0)-\Sigma_{+-}^{(KK;z_0)}.
}
\]

In the pure-even residual subbranch \(\Lambda_O^{(0)}=0\), this simplifies to
\[
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{++}^{EE},
}
\]
\[
\boxed{
d_-^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{--}^{EE},
}
\]
\[
\boxed{
m_0
=
B_{z_0}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}.
}
\]

So the same-shell benchmark-side frontier has now been reduced to the finite overlap data
\[
\boxed{
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0),\quad
B_{z_0}(0),\quad
\mathcal S_{++}^{EE},\quad
\mathcal S_{--}^{EE},\quad
\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}
}
\]
in the explicit pure-even residual realization.

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\section{Pure-Even \(KK\) Residual Reduction and a Practical Same-Shell Benchmark Inequality}

\section{Short explanation}

For the explicit branch
\[
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \eta=z_0,
\]
the same-shell non-enriched residual is purely \(KK\).
If we further specialize to the pure-even residual subbranch
\[
\Lambda_O^{(0)}=0,
\]
then the entire same-shell benchmark is controlled by the three finite overlap sums
\[
\mathcal S_{++}^{EE},\qquad
\mathcal S_{--}^{EE},\qquad
\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}.
\]

Under an additional valley-symmetric residual assumption
\[
\mathcal S_{++}^{EE}=\mathcal S_{--}^{EE}=:\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE},
\]
the zero-momentum same-shell benchmark reduces to a single scalar inequality.

\section{1. Pure-even residual coefficients}

From the \(K\)-sector defect ansatz and the already established \(JJ=JK=0\) result on the \(z_0\)-slot, the zero-momentum same-shell coefficients are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{++}^{EE},
}
\label{eq:pe_dplus}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_-^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{--}^{EE},
}
\label{eq:pe_dminus}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_0
=
B_{z_0}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}.
}
\label{eq:pe_m0}
\end{equation}

Introduce the shorthand
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
a_K
:=
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2.
}
\label{eq:pe_aK}
\end{equation}
Then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}=E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)-a_K\mathcal S_{++}^{EE},
\qquad
d_-^{(0)}=E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)-a_K\mathcal S_{--}^{EE},
\qquad
m_0=B_{z_0}(0)-a_K\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}.
}
\label{eq:pe_compact}
\end{equation}

\section{2. Valley-symmetric residual subcase}

Assume
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{++}^{EE}=\mathcal S_{--}^{EE}=:\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}.
}
\label{eq:pe_valley_sym}
\end{equation}
Then the diagonal entries are equal:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}=d_-^{(0)}=:d^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)-a_K\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}.
}
\label{eq:pe_dequal}
\end{equation}
Hence the exact zero-momentum eigenvalues are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\lambda_\pm(0)
=
d^{(0)}\pm |m_0|.
}
\label{eq:pe_eigs}
\end{equation}
Therefore the exact zero-momentum same-shell benchmark is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},0}^{(1)}
=
\left|
\,
\left|E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)-a_K\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}\right|
-
\left|B_{z_0}(0)-a_K\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}\right|
\right|.
}
\label{eq:pe_gap_exact}
\end{equation}

A sufficient condition for positivity is therefore
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\left|E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)-a_K\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}\right|
>
\left|B_{z_0}(0)-a_K\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}\right|.
}
\label{eq:pe_gap_suff_exact}
\end{equation}

\section{3. Cauchy--Schwarz control of the off-diagonal overlap}

By Cauchy--Schwarz, the off-diagonal overlap obeys
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}|^2
\le
\mathcal S_{++}^{EE}\mathcal S_{--}^{EE}.
}
\label{eq:pe_CS}
\end{equation}
In the valley-symmetric subcase \eqref{eq:pe_valley_sym},
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}|
\le
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}.
}
\label{eq:pe_CS_sym}
\end{equation}

Therefore
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\left|B_{z_0}(0)-a_K\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}\right|
\le
|B_{z_0}(0)|+a_K\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE},
}
\label{eq:pe_upper_m}
\end{equation}
while
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\left|E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)-a_K\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}\right|
\ge
|E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)|-a_K\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}.
}
\label{eq:pe_lower_d}
\end{equation}

Hence a stronger but easier sufficient condition is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)|-|B_{z_0}(0)|
>
2a_K\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}.
}
\label{eq:pe_gap_suff_simple}
\end{equation}

This is a purely scalar practical bound.

\section{4. Insertion of the direct locked-core part}

The direct locked-core part has already been reduced to
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
=
\omega_B(k_*)+12uA^2+\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(0)\bigr]_{z_0z_0},
}
\label{eq:pe_Edir}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
B_{z_0}(0)
=
4uA^2+\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(G_*)\bigr]_{z_0z_0},
}
\label{eq:pe_Bdir}
\end{equation}
with
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\omega_B(k_*)
=
-\mu^2+\frac{Zq_*^2}{4}-\frac{Yq_*^4}{16}.
}
\label{eq:pe_omega}
\end{equation}

Therefore the practical sufficient condition \eqref{eq:pe_gap_suff_simple} becomes
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\left|
\omega_B(k_*)+12uA^2+\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(0)\bigr]_{z_0z_0}
\right|
-
\left|
4uA^2+\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(G_*)\bigr]_{z_0z_0}
\right|
>
2\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}.
}
\label{eq:pe_final_suff}
\end{equation}

\section{5. Minimal scalar-only locked-core subcase}

If no additional direct locked-line refinement is switched on, then
\[
\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(0)\bigr]_{z_0z_0}=0,
\qquad
\bigl[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(G_*)\bigr]_{z_0z_0}=0.
\]
Hence
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)=\omega_B(k_*)+12uA^2,
\qquad
B_{z_0}(0)=4uA^2.
}
\label{eq:pe_minimal_direct}
\end{equation}

Then the practical same-shell sufficient condition becomes
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\left|
\omega_B(k_*)+12uA^2
\right|
-
4uA^2
>
2\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}.
}
\label{eq:pe_minimal_suff}
\end{equation}

If, moreover,
\[
u>0,
\qquad
\omega_B(k_*)+12uA^2\ge 0,
\]
then \eqref{eq:pe_minimal_suff} simplifies to
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\omega_B(k_*)+8uA^2
>
2\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}.
}
\label{eq:pe_minimal_simplest}
\end{equation}

This is the cleanest explicit same-shell benchmark inequality now available for the branch.

\section{6. Insertion into the final remote-gap benchmark}

The same-shell usable benchmark entry is
\[
