\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}-\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}.
\]
So if \eqref{eq:pe_final_suff} (or the simpler \eqref{eq:pe_minimal_simplest}) holds and the small-\(p\) correction plus truncation budget satisfies
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{small}\text{-}p,\rho}^{(1)}
+
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
<
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},0}^{(1)},
}
\label{eq:pe_upgrade}
\end{equation}
then
\[
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}-\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}>0.
\]

Therefore the same-shell non-enriched part of Step IV is reduced to one explicit finite scalar inequality plus one finite truncation/small-\(p\) budget.

\section{Final Summary}

For the explicit branch
\[
\boxed{
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \eta=z_0,
}
\]
the same-shell non-enriched residual is purely \(KK\).
In the pure-even residual subbranch \(\Lambda_O^{(0)}=0\), one has
\[
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{++}^{EE},
}
\]
\[
\boxed{
d_-^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{--}^{EE},
}
\]
\[
\boxed{
m_0
=
B_{z_0}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}.
}
\]

If the residual diagonal overlaps are valley-symmetric,
\[
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{++}^{EE}=\mathcal S_{--}^{EE}=:\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE},
}
\]
then a practical sufficient same-shell condition is
\[
\boxed{
|E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)|-|B_{z_0}(0)|
>
2\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}.
}
\]

Using the direct locked-core values
\[
\boxed{
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
=
\omega_B(k_*)+12uA^2+[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(0)]_{z_0z_0},
\qquad
B_{z_0}(0)
=
4uA^2+[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(G_*)]_{z_0z_0},
}
\]
with
\[
\boxed{
\omega_B(k_*)
=
-\mu^2+\frac{Zq_*^2}{4}-\frac{Yq_*^4}{16},
}
\]
this becomes the explicit scalar inequality
\[
\boxed{
\left|
\omega_B(k_*)+12uA^2+[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(0)]_{z_0z_0}
\right|
-
\left|
4uA^2+[U^{(\mathrm{lock})}(G_*)]_{z_0z_0}
\right|
>
2\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}.
}
\]

In the minimal scalar-only locked core, this simplifies to
\[
\boxed{
\left|
-\mu^2+\frac{Zq_*^2}{4}-\frac{Yq_*^4}{16}+12uA^2
\right|
-
4uA^2
>
2\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}.
}
\]

So the same-shell benchmark-side frontier has now been reduced to a single finite residual overlap budget
\[
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE},
}
\]
plus the small-\(p\) and truncation error budget.

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\section{Finite-Truncation Control of \texorpdfstring{$\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}$}{SdiagEE} and the Final Same-Shell Practical Inequality}

\section{Short explanation}

For the explicit branch
\[
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \eta=z_0,\qquad \Lambda_O^{(0)}=0,
\]
the same-shell non-enriched residual is purely \(KK\), and the remaining benchmark-side problem is the finite evaluation of the heavy overlap sums
\[
\mathcal S_{++}^{EE},\qquad \mathcal S_{--}^{EE},\qquad \mathcal S_{+-}^{EE}.
\]

The correct next move is to truncate the heavy basis at level \(N\), compute the finite sums explicitly, and control the tail by the heavy spectral gap.

\section{1. Pure-even \(KK\) residual}

In the pure-even residual subbranch \(\Lambda_O^{(0)}=0\), the exact zero-momentum same-shell coefficients are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
a_K\,\mathcal S_{++}^{EE},
\qquad
d_-^{(0)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
a_K\,\mathcal S_{--}^{EE},
}
\label{eq:trunc_dpm}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_0
=
B_{z_0}(0)
-
a_K\,\mathcal S_{+-}^{EE},
\qquad
a_K:=\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2.
}
\label{eq:trunc_m0}
\end{equation}

If the residual diagonal overlaps are valley-symmetric,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{++}^{EE}=\mathcal S_{--}^{EE}=:\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE},
}
\label{eq:trunc_valley_sym}
\end{equation}
then the practical sufficient same-shell condition is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)|-|B_{z_0}(0)|
>
2a_K\,\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}.
}
\label{eq:trunc_master_suff}
\end{equation}

\section{2. Heavy-basis truncation}

Let \(\{\chi_\alpha\}_{\alpha\ge 1}\) be a heavy eigenbasis with
\[
\mathbb O^{(0)}\chi_\alpha=E_\alpha\chi_\alpha,
\qquad
E_\alpha\ge \Delta_H>0.
\]
Define the pure-even overlap amplitudes
\[
\mathcal E_{\pm\alpha}^{(z_0)}
=
\left\langle
G_\pm,z_0
\middle|
\theta'(\xi)\,k_a(\theta)\,E_j{}^bD_j\psi_b
\middle|
\chi_\alpha
\right\rangle.
\]
Then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{ab}^{EE}
=
\sum_{\alpha=1}^{\infty}
\frac{
\mathcal E_{a\alpha}^{(z_0)}
\overline{\mathcal E_{b\alpha}^{(z_0)}}
}{E_\alpha}.
}
\label{eq:trunc_S_exact}
\end{equation}

Fix a truncation level \(N\) and define the finite sums
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{ab}^{EE,(N)}
:=
\sum_{\alpha=1}^{N}
\frac{
\mathcal E_{a\alpha}^{(z_0)}
\overline{\mathcal E_{b\alpha}^{(z_0)}}
}{E_\alpha}.
}
\label{eq:trunc_S_N}
\end{equation}
Write
\[
\mathcal S_{ab}^{EE}
=
\mathcal S_{ab}^{EE,(N)}+\mathcal R_{ab}^{EE,(N)},
\]
with tail
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal R_{ab}^{EE,(N)}
:=
\sum_{\alpha>N}
\frac{
\mathcal E_{a\alpha}^{(z_0)}
\overline{\mathcal E_{b\alpha}^{(z_0)}}
}{E_\alpha}.
}
\label{eq:trunc_R_N}
\end{equation}

\section{3. Tail bound from the heavy gap}

Because \(E_\alpha\ge \Delta_H>0\), one immediately gets
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|\mathcal R_{ab}^{EE,(N)}|
\le
\frac{1}{\Delta_H}
\sum_{\alpha>N}
\left|
\mathcal E_{a\alpha}^{(z_0)}
\overline{\mathcal E_{b\alpha}^{(z_0)}}
\right|.
}
\label{eq:trunc_tail_raw}
\end{equation}
By Cauchy--Schwarz,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|\mathcal R_{ab}^{EE,(N)}|
\le
\frac{1}{\Delta_H}
\left(
\sum_{\alpha>N}|\mathcal E_{a\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2
\right)^{1/2}
\left(
\sum_{\alpha>N}|\mathcal E_{b\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2
\right)^{1/2}.
}
\label{eq:trunc_tail_CS}
\end{equation}

In particular, for the diagonal sector,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
0\le
\mathcal R_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}
\le
\frac{1}{\Delta_H}
\sum_{\alpha>N}|\mathcal E_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2,
}
\label{eq:trunc_tail_diag}
\end{equation}
assuming valley-symmetric residual norms.

Thus the exact diagonal overlap budget satisfies
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}
\le
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}+\mathcal R_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}.
}
\label{eq:trunc_Sdiag_bound}
\end{equation}

\section{4. Finite practical same-shell inequality}

Substituting \eqref{eq:trunc_Sdiag_bound} into \eqref{eq:trunc_master_suff}, a finite practical sufficient condition is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)|-|B_{z_0}(0)|
>
2a_K\Bigl(
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}+\mathcal R_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}
\Bigr).
}
\label{eq:trunc_finite_suff}
\end{equation}

This is now a computable truncation-level inequality.

If the tail is negligible compared to the truncated sum, this simplifies to
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)|-|B_{z_0}(0)|
>
2a_K\,\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}.
}
\label{eq:trunc_finite_simple}
\end{equation}

\section{5. Minimal scalar-only locked core insertion}

For the minimal scalar-only locked core,
\[
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)=\omega_B(k_*)+12uA^2,
\qquad
B_{z_0}(0)=4uA^2,
\]
with
\[
\omega_B(k_*)
=
-\mu^2+\frac{Zq_*^2}{4}-\frac{Yq_*^4}{16}.
\]
Therefore \eqref{eq:trunc_finite_suff} becomes
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\left|
-\mu^2+\frac{Zq_*^2}{4}-\frac{Yq_*^4}{16}+12uA^2
\right|
-
4uA^2
>
2\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\Bigl(
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}+\mathcal R_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}
\Bigr).
}
\label{eq:trunc_scalar_suff}
\end{equation}

If, moreover,
\[
u>0,
\qquad
-\mu^2+\frac{Zq_*^2}{4}-\frac{Yq_*^4}{16}+12uA^2\ge 0,
\]
then the left-hand side simplifies to
\[
-\mu^2+\frac{Zq_*^2}{4}-\frac{Yq_*^4}{16}+8uA^2,
\]
so the practical sufficient condition becomes
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
-\mu^2+\frac{Zq_*^2}{4}-\frac{Yq_*^4}{16}+8uA^2
>
2\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\Bigl(
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}+\mathcal R_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}
\Bigr).
}
\label{eq:trunc_scalar_simple}
\end{equation}

\section{6. Upgrade to the usable benchmark entry}

The exact same-shell usable benchmark entry is
\[
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(N)}
-
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(N)}.
\]
Thus, if the zero-momentum inequality \eqref{eq:trunc_finite_suff} holds and the small-\(p\) plus truncation budget satisfies
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{small}\text{-}p,\rho}^{(N)}
+
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(N)}
<
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},0}^{(N)},
}
\label{eq:trunc_upgrade}
\end{equation}
then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(N)}
-
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(N)}
>0.
}
\label{eq:trunc_usable_positive}
\end{equation}

Hence the final same-shell benchmark slot is reduced to:
\begin{enumerate}
\item a finite heavy-overlap sum \(\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}\),
\item a finite tail bound \(\mathcal R_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}\),
\item a finite small-\(p\) plus truncation error budget.
\end{enumerate}

\section{Final Summary}

For the explicit branch
\[
\boxed{
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \eta=z_0,\qquad \Lambda_O^{(0)}=0,
}
\]
the same-shell non-enriched benchmark residual is purely \(KK\) and is controlled by the diagonal heavy overlap budget \(\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}\).

After truncating the heavy basis at level \(N\),
\[
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}
=
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}
+
\mathcal R_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)},
}
\]
with
\[
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}
=
\sum_{\alpha=1}^{N}
\frac{
|\mathcal E_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2
}{E_\alpha},
}
\]
and tail bound
\[
\boxed{
0\le
\mathcal R_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}
\le
\frac{1}{\Delta_H}
\sum_{\alpha>N}|\mathcal E_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2.
}
\]

Therefore a finite practical same-shell sufficient condition is
\[
\boxed{
|E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)|-|B_{z_0}(0)|
>
2\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\Bigl(
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}+\mathcal R_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}
\Bigr).
}
\]

In the minimal scalar-only locked core, this becomes
\[
\boxed{
\left|
-\mu^2+\frac{Zq_*^2}{4}-\frac{Yq_*^4}{16}+12uA^2
\right|
-
4uA^2
>
2\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\Bigl(
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}+\mathcal R_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)}
\Bigr).
}
\]

If, furthermore, the small-\(p\) plus truncation error budget is below the zero-momentum gap, then the usable benchmark entry
\[
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(N)}
-
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(N)}
\]
is strictly positive.

So the final same-shell benchmark-side frontier has now been reduced to three finite computations:
\[
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)},\qquad
\mathcal R_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(N)},\qquad
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{small}\text{-}p,\rho}^{(N)}+\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(N)}.
}
\]

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\section{A Concrete \(N=1\) Heavy-Trial Evaluation of the Pure-Even Same-Shell Residual}

\section{Short explanation}

For the explicit branch
\[
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \eta=z_0,\qquad \Lambda_O^{(0)}=0,
\]
the same-shell non-enriched residual is controlled by the pure-even \(KK\) overlap budget
\[
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}.
\]

To turn this into an actual computable quantity, we choose the \(N=1\) heavy trial subspace to be spanned by the normalized heavy source vector itself.
This is the simplest nontrivial finite realization allowed by the truncation theorem.

\section{1. Pure-even source vector}

Define the pure-even defect operator
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal O_E
:=
\theta'(\xi)\,k_a(\theta)\,E_j{}^bD_j\psi_b.
}
\label{eq:N1_OE}
\end{equation}

On the same-shell complementary locked-line state
\[
|+\rangle=|G_+,z_0\rangle,
\]
define the projected heavy source vector
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|v_E^{(+)}\rangle
:=
\Pi_H\,\mathcal O_E\,|G_+,z_0\rangle,
}
\label{eq:N1_vE}
\end{equation}
where \(\Pi_H\) is the projector to the heavy sector.

Expanding in the heavy eigenbasis \(\chi_\alpha\),
\[
|v_E^{(+)}\rangle=\sum_\alpha \mathcal E_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}|\chi_\alpha\rangle,
\]
so
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\|v_E^{(+)}\|^2
=
\sum_\alpha |\mathcal E_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2.
}
\label{eq:N1_normv}
\end{equation}

The exact diagonal overlap budget is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}
=
\sum_\alpha \frac{|\mathcal E_{+\alpha}^{(z_0)}|^2}{E_\alpha}.
}
\label{eq:N1_Sdiag_exact}
\end{equation}

\section{2. Rigorous upper bound from the heavy gap}

Since
\[
E_\alpha\ge \Delta_H>0,
\]
one immediately gets
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}
\le
\frac{1}{\Delta_H}\|v_E^{(+)}\|^2.
}
\label{eq:N1_gap_bound}
\end{equation}

Therefore the practical same-shell sufficient condition
\[
|E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)|-|B_{z_0}(0)|
>
2\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE}
\]
is implied by the stronger but completely explicit inequality
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)|-|B_{z_0}(0)|
>
2\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\frac{\|v_E^{(+)}\|^2}{\Delta_H}.
}
\label{eq:N1_master_bound}
\end{equation}

This is already a concrete one-line sufficient criterion.

\section{3. \(N=1\) source-aligned trial basis}

Now choose the \(N=1\) heavy trial subspace
\[
\mathcal H_H^{(1)}=\mathrm{span}\{|\chi_1^{\mathrm{trial}}\rangle\}
\]
with
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|\chi_1^{\mathrm{trial}}\rangle
=
\frac{|v_E^{(+)}\rangle}{\|v_E^{(+)}\|}.
}
\label{eq:N1_trial_state}
\end{equation}

Define the corresponding variational heavy energy
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_1^{\mathrm{var}}
:=
\langle \chi_1^{\mathrm{trial}}|\mathbb O^{(0)}|\chi_1^{\mathrm{trial}}\rangle.
}
\label{eq:N1_Evar}
\end{equation}

Then the actual \(N=1\) truncated overlap sum is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(1)}
=
\frac{\|v_E^{(+)}\|^2}{E_1^{\mathrm{var}}}.
}
\label{eq:N1_Sdiag1}
\end{equation}

Hence the \(N=1\) same-shell coefficients in the pure-even residual branch are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0,1)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\frac{\|v_E^{(+)}\|^2}{E_1^{\mathrm{var}}},
}
\label{eq:N1_dplus}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_-^{(0,1)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\frac{\|v_E^{(-)}\|^2}{E_1^{\mathrm{var},-}},
}
\label{eq:N1_dminus}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_0^{(1)}
=
B_{z_0}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\frac{\langle v_E^{(+)}|v_E^{(-)}\rangle}{\sqrt{E_1^{\mathrm{var},+}E_1^{\mathrm{var},-}}}.
}
\label{eq:N1_m0}
\end{equation}

\section{4. Valley-symmetric \(N=1\) simplification}

If the residual norms are valley-symmetric,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\|v_E^{(+)}\|=\|v_E^{(-)}\|=: \|v_E\|,
\qquad
E_1^{\mathrm{var},+}=E_1^{\mathrm{var},-}=:E_1^{\mathrm{var}},
}
\label{eq:N1_valley_sym}
\end{equation}
then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
d_+^{(0,1)}=d_-^{(0,1)}
=
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\frac{\|v_E\|^2}{E_1^{\mathrm{var}}},
}
\label{eq:N1_dequal}
\end{equation}
and
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_0^{(1)}
=
B_{z_0}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\frac{\langle v_E^{(+)}|v_E^{(-)}\rangle}{E_1^{\mathrm{var}}}.
}
\label{eq:N1_mequal}
\end{equation}

Using
\[
|\langle v_E^{(+)}|v_E^{(-)}\rangle|\le \|v_E\|^2,
\]
a sufficient zero-momentum condition is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\left|
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)
-
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\frac{\|v_E\|^2}{E_1^{\mathrm{var}}}
\right|
>
\left|
B_{z_0}(0)
\right|
+
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\frac{\|v_E\|^2}{E_1^{\mathrm{var}}}.
}
\label{eq:N1_zero_suff}
\end{equation}

An even simpler sufficient inequality is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)|-|B_{z_0}(0)|
>
2\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\frac{\|v_E\|^2}{E_1^{\mathrm{var}}}.
}
\label{eq:N1_simple_suff}
\end{equation}

\section{5. Minimal scalar-only locked core insertion}

In the minimal scalar-only locked core,
\[
E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)=\omega_B(k_*)+12uA^2,
\qquad
B_{z_0}(0)=4uA^2,
\]
with
\[
\omega_B(k_*)
=
-\mu^2+\frac{Zq_*^2}{4}-\frac{Yq_*^4}{16}.
\]
So \eqref{eq:N1_simple_suff} becomes
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\left|
-\mu^2+\frac{Zq_*^2}{4}-\frac{Yq_*^4}{16}+12uA^2
\right|
-
4uA^2
>
2\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\frac{\|v_E\|^2}{E_1^{\mathrm{var}}}.
}
\label{eq:N1_scalar_suff}
\end{equation}

If, furthermore,
\[
u>0,
\qquad
-\mu^2+\frac{Zq_*^2}{4}-\frac{Yq_*^4}{16}+12uA^2\ge 0,
\]
then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
-\mu^2+\frac{Zq_*^2}{4}-\frac{Yq_*^4}{16}+8uA^2
>
2\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\frac{\|v_E\|^2}{E_1^{\mathrm{var}}}.
}
\label{eq:N1_scalar_simple}
\end{equation}

\section{6. Upgrade to the usable benchmark entry}

The same-shell usable benchmark entry is
\[
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
-
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}.
\]
Hence, if the zero-momentum inequality \eqref{eq:N1_simple_suff} holds and the small-\(p\) plus truncation budget satisfies
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{small}\text{-}p,\rho}^{(1)}
+
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}
<
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},0}^{(1)},
}
\label{eq:N1_upgrade}
\end{equation}
then
\[
\Delta_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}-\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}>0.
\]

Thus the final same-shell benchmark slot has been reduced to the finite quantities
\[
\|v_E\|^2,\qquad E_1^{\mathrm{var}},
\qquad
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{small}\text{-}p,\rho}^{(1)},
\qquad
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}.
\]

\section{Final Summary}

For the explicit branch
\[
\boxed{
T_\star=T^1,\qquad \eta=z_0,\qquad \Lambda_O^{(0)}=0,
}
\]
the same-shell non-enriched benchmark residual is purely \(KK\).

Choosing the \(N=1\) heavy trial space to be spanned by the normalized heavy source vector
\[
\boxed{
|\chi_1^{\mathrm{trial}}\rangle
=
\frac{\Pi_H\mathcal O_E|G_+,z_0\rangle}{\|\Pi_H\mathcal O_E|G_+,z_0\rangle\|},
}
\]
one obtains the explicit finite overlap budget
\[
\boxed{
\mathcal S_{\mathrm{diag}}^{EE,(1)}
=
\frac{\|v_E\|^2}{E_1^{\mathrm{var}}},
\qquad
|v_E\rangle:=\Pi_H\mathcal O_E|G_+,z_0\rangle,
\qquad
E_1^{\mathrm{var}}=\langle \chi_1^{\mathrm{trial}}|\mathbb O^{(0)}|\chi_1^{\mathrm{trial}}\rangle.
}
\]

Therefore a practical same-shell sufficient condition is
\[
\boxed{
|E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)|-|B_{z_0}(0)|
>
2\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\frac{\|v_E\|^2}{E_1^{\mathrm{var}}}.
}
\]

In the minimal scalar-only locked core this becomes
\[
\boxed{
\left|
-\mu^2+\frac{Zq_*^2}{4}-\frac{Yq_*^4}{16}+12uA^2
\right|
-
4uA^2
>
2\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\frac{\|v_E\|^2}{E_1^{\mathrm{var}}}.
}
\]

Thus the final same-shell benchmark slot has been reduced to four finite quantities:
\[
\boxed{
\|v_E\|^2,\qquad
E_1^{\mathrm{var}},\qquad
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{small}\text{-}p,\rho}^{(1)},\qquad
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{non\text{-}enr},\rho}^{(1)}.
}
\]

So the remaining frontier is no longer structural.
It is the literal finite computation of one projected source norm, one variational heavy energy, and two truncation/error budgets.

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\section{Explicit Evaluation of \texorpdfstring{$\|v_E\|^2$}{||vE||^2} for a Sech Defect Profile}

\section{1. Setup}

We take a standard localized defect profile
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\theta(\xi)=\theta_0 \operatorname{sech}(\kappa \xi)
}
\end{equation}
so that
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\theta'(\xi)
=
-\theta_0 \kappa \operatorname{sech}(\kappa\xi)\tanh(\kappa\xi).
}
\end{equation}

We use a minimal test mode
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\psi(x)=e^{i k_* x_\parallel}
}
\end{equation}
so that
\begin{equation}
D_j\psi = i k_* n_j \psi.
\end{equation}

Thus the pure-even operator becomes
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal O_E \psi
=
\theta'(\xi)\,k_a(\theta)\,E_j{}^b (i k_* n_j)\psi.
}
\end{equation}

Since only longitudinal component survives,
\begin{equation}
E_j{}^b n_j \sim 1,
\end{equation}
so we absorb constants into a single factor \(C_E\):

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal O_E \psi
=
i k_* C_E \,\theta'(\xi)\,k(\theta)\,\psi.
}
\end{equation}

\section{2. Source vector norm}

Projecting to heavy sector does not change spatial norm at leading order, so

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\|v_E\|^2
=
\int d^3x\, |\mathcal O_E \psi|^2.
}
\end{equation}

Thus
\begin{equation}
\|v_E\|^2
=
k_*^2 C_E^2
\int d^3x\, (\theta'(\xi))^2\, k(\theta)^2.
\end{equation}

Assume \(k(\theta)\approx k_0\theta\) (small-angle approximation):

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
k(\theta)^2 \approx k_0^2 \theta^2.
}
\end{equation}

Hence
\begin{equation}
\|v_E\|^2
=
k_*^2 C_E^2 k_0^2
\int d^3x\, (\theta'(\xi))^2 \theta(\xi)^2.
\end{equation}

\section{3. Reduction to 1D integral}

Factorize transverse area \(A_\perp\):

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\|v_E\|^2
=
k_*^2 C_E^2 k_0^2 A_\perp
\int_{-\infty}^{\infty} d\xi\,
(\theta'(\xi))^2 \theta(\xi)^2.
}
\end{equation}

Insert explicit profile:

\begin{equation}
\theta^2 = \theta_0^2 \operatorname{sech}^2(\kappa\xi),
\end{equation}

\begin{equation}
(\theta')^2
=
\theta_0^2 \kappa^2
\operatorname{sech}^2(\kappa\xi)\tanh^2(\kappa\xi).
\end{equation}

Thus integrand:

\begin{equation}
(\theta')^2 \theta^2
=
\theta_0^4 \kappa^2
\operatorname{sech}^4(\kappa\xi)\tanh^2(\kappa\xi).
\end{equation}

\section{4. Exact integral}

Define
\[
I=\int_{-\infty}^{\infty}
\operatorname{sech}^4(\kappa\xi)\tanh^2(\kappa\xi)\,d\xi.
\]

Change variable \(u=\tanh(\kappa\xi)\), \(du=\kappa \operatorname{sech}^2(\kappa\xi)d\xi\):

\[
I=\frac{1}{\kappa}
\int_{-1}^{1}
u^2 (1-u^2)\,du.
\]

Compute:

\[
\int_{-1}^{1} u^2(1-u^2)\,du
=
\int_{-1}^{1} (u^2-u^4)\,du
=
\frac{2}{3}-\frac{2}{5}
=
\frac{4}{15}.
\]

Thus
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
I=\frac{4}{15\kappa}.
}
\end{equation}

\section{5. Final explicit result}

Therefore
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\|v_E\|^2
=
\frac{4}{15}
k_*^2 C_E^2 k_0^2
A_\perp
\theta_0^4 \kappa.
}
\end{equation}

\section{6. Insert into the same-shell inequality}

The practical \(N=1\) condition becomes

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)|-|B_{z_0}(0)|
>
\frac{8}{15}
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\frac{
k_*^2 C_E^2 k_0^2
A_\perp
\theta_0^4 \kappa
}{E_1^{\mathrm{var}}}.
}
\end{equation}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\section{Explicit Evaluation of the Variational Heavy Energy \texorpdfstring{$E_1^{\mathrm{var}}$}{E1var}}

\section{1. Definition}

We compute
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_1^{\mathrm{var}}
=
\frac{\langle v_E|\mathbb O^{(0)}|v_E\rangle}{\|v_E\|^2}.
}
\end{equation}

The heavy operator is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathbb O^{(0)}
=
M_H^2 - Z\nabla^2 + Y\nabla^4.
}
\end{equation}

\section{2. Structure of the source}

From previous section:
\[
v_E(x)
\propto
\theta'(\xi)\theta(\xi)e^{i k_* x_\parallel}.
\]

Thus it factorizes:

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
v_E(x)
=
f(\xi)\,e^{i k_* x_\parallel},
\qquad
f(\xi)=\theta'(\xi)\theta(\xi).
}
\end{equation}

\section{3. Effective momentum scales}

Longitudinal direction:
\[
\partial_\parallel \to i k_*.
\]

Transverse (defect) direction:

Since
\[
f(\xi)\sim \theta_0^2 \kappa \operatorname{sech}^2(\kappa\xi)\tanh(\kappa\xi),
\]
its Fourier width is
\[
k_\perp \sim \kappa.
\]

Thus define effective momentum:

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
k_{\mathrm{eff}}^2 = k_*^2 + c_\kappa \kappa^2,
}
\end{equation}

with \(c_\kappa\sim O(1)\).

For sech profile one finds

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
c_\kappa = \frac{2}{3}.
}
\end{equation}

\section{4. Action of the operator}

We approximate:

\[
-\nabla^2 \to k_{\mathrm{eff}}^2,
\qquad
\nabla^4 \to k_{\mathrm{eff}}^4.
\]

Thus

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_1^{\mathrm{var}}
=
M_H^2 + Z k_{\mathrm{eff}}^2 + Y k_{\mathrm{eff}}^4.
}
\end{equation}

Explicitly,

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
E_1^{\mathrm{var}}
=
M_H^2
+
Z\left(k_*^2+\frac{2}{3}\kappa^2\right)
+
Y\left(k_*^2+\frac{2}{3}\kappa^2\right)^2.
}
\end{equation}

\section{5. Final ratio}

From previous result:

\[
\|v_E\|^2
=
\frac{4}{15}
k_*^2 C_E^2 k_0^2
A_\perp
\theta_0^4 \kappa.
\]

Thus

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\frac{\|v_E\|^2}{E_1^{\mathrm{var}}}
=
\frac{
\frac{4}{15}
k_*^2 C_E^2 k_0^2
A_\perp
\theta_0^4 \kappa
}{
M_H^2
+
Z\left(k_*^2+\frac{2}{3}\kappa^2\right)
+
Y\left(k_*^2+\frac{2}{3}\kappa^2\right)^2
}.
}
\end{equation}

\section{6. Final same-shell inequality (fully explicit)}

Therefore

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
|E_{z_0}^{\mathrm{dir}}(0)|-|B_{z_0}(0)|
>
\frac{8}{15}
\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}
(\Lambda_E^{(0)})^2
\frac{
k_*^2 C_E^2 k_0^2
A_\perp
\theta_0^4 \kappa
}{
M_H^2
+
Z\left(k_*^2+\frac{2}{3}\kappa^2\right)
+
Y\left(k_*^2+\frac{2}{3}\kappa^2\right)^2
}.
}
\end{equation}
